国家与革命

State and Revolution





六世·列宁 

V. I. Lenin 

第一版序言

Preface to the First Edition

国家问题如今在理论和政治实践中都变得尤为重要。帝国主义战争极大地加速和加剧了垄断资本主义向国家垄断资本主义的转变进程。国家对劳动人民的残酷压迫日益加剧，而国家本身也与权力无所不能的资本家集团日益融合。发达国家——我们指的是它们的腹地——正在沦为工人的军事监狱。

The question of the state is now acquiring particular importance both in theory and in practical politics. The imperialist war has immensely accelerated and intensified the process of transformation of monopoly capitalism into state-monopoly capitalism. The monstrous oppression of the working people by the state, which is merging more and more with the all-powerful capitalist associations, is becoming increasingly monstrous. The advanced countries - we mean their hinterland - are becoming military convict prisons for the workers.

旷日持久的战争带来的前所未有的恐怖和苦难，使人民的处境变得难以忍受，激起了他们的愤怒。世界无产阶级革命显然正在走向成熟。革命与国家的关系问题正变得具有现实意义。

The unprecedented horrors and miseries of the protracted was are making the people's position unbearable and increasing their anger. The world proletarian revolution is clearly maturing. The question of its relation to the state is acquiring practical importance.

在数十年相对和平的发展过程中积累的机会主义因素，催生了社会沙文主义的潮流，这种潮流主导了世界各地的官方社会主义政党。这种潮流——口是社会主义，实则是沙文主义（例如俄国的普列汉诺夫、波特列索夫、布列什科夫斯卡娅、鲁巴诺维奇，以及略加掩饰的采列捷利、切尔诺夫等人；德国的谢德曼、莱吉安、戴维等人；法国和比利时的雷诺德尔、盖斯德和范德维尔德；英国的海因德曼和费边社等等）——其显著特征是“社会主义领导人”卑躬屈膝地迎合“他们”的民族资产阶级利益，以及“他们”的国家利益，因为大多数所谓的大国长期以来一直在剥削和奴役众多弱小国家。帝国主义战争就是一场瓜分和再瓜分这种战利品的战争。如果不反对有关“国家”的机会主义偏见，就不可能将劳动人民从资产阶级，特别是帝国主义资产阶级的影响下解放出来。

The elements of opportunism that accumulated over the decades of comparatively peaceful development have given rise to the trend of social-chauvinism which dominated the official socialist parties throughout the world. This trend - socialism in words and chauvinism in deeds (Plekhanov, Potresov, Breshkovskaya, Rubanovich, and, in a slightly veiled form, Tsereteli, Chernov and Co. in Russia; Scheidemann. Legien, David and others in Germany; Renaudel, Guesde and Vandervelde in France and Belgium; Hyndman and the Fabians in England, etc., etc.) - is conspicuous for the base, servile adaptation of the "leaders of socialism" to the interests not only of "their" national bourgeoisie, but of "their" state, for the majority of the so-called Great Powers have long been exploiting and enslaving a whole number of small and weak nations. And the imperialist war is a war for the division and redivision of this kind of booty. The struggle to free the working people from the influence of the bourgeoisie in general, and of the imperialist bourgeoisie in particular, is impossible without a struggle against opportunist prejudices concerning the "state".

首先，我们考察马克思和恩格斯的国家理论，并着重探讨该理论中被机会主义者忽视或歪曲的方面。然后，我们重点论述造成这些歪曲的主要责任人——第二国际（1889-1914）最著名的领导人卡尔·考茨基，该组织在当前的战争中遭遇了惨重的失败。最后，我们总结1905年俄国革命，特别是1917年俄国革命的主要成果。表面上看，后者（1917年8月初）正处于其发展的第一阶段；但这场革命整体上只能被理解为帝国主义战争引发的一系列社会主义无产阶级革命中的一环。因此，社会主义无产阶级革命与国家的关系问题不仅具有实际的政治意义，而且具有当今最紧迫问题的意义，即向群众解释他们不久将要做什么才能摆脱资本主义暴政的问题。

First of all we examine the theory of Marx and Engels of the state, and dwell in particular detail on those aspects of this theory which are ignored or have been distorted by the opportunists. Then we deal specially with the one who is chiefly responsible for these distortions, Karl Kautsky, the best-known leader of the Second International (1889-1914), which has met with such miserable bankruptcy in the present war. Lastly, we sum up the main results of the experience of the Russian revolutions of 1905 and particularly of 1917. Apparently, the latter is now (early August 1917) completing the first stage of its development; but this revolution as a whole can only be understood as a link in a chain of socialist proletarian revolutions being caused by the imperialist war. The question of the relation of the socialist proletarian revolution to the state, therefore, is acquiring not only practical political importance, but also the significance of a most urgent problem of the day, the problem of explaining to the masses what they will have to do before long to free themselves from capitalist tyranny.

作者

1917年8月

The Author

August 1917









第二版序言

Preface to the Second Edition

目前的第二版基本保持不变，只是在第二章中增加了第三节。

The present, second edition is published virtually unaltered, except that section 3 had been added to Chapter II.

作者：

莫斯科

，1918年12月17日

The Author

Moscow

December 17, 1918





阶级社会与国家

Class Society and the State

国家：阶级对抗不可调和的产物

The State: a Product of the Irreconcilability of Class Antagonisms

武装人员特遣队、监狱等等。

国家：剥削被压迫阶级的工具。

“国家的消亡”与暴力革命

Special Bodies of Armed Men, Prisons, etc.

The State: an Instrument for the Exploitation of the Oppressed Class

The "Withering Away" of the State, and Violent Revolution



 



 

1. 国家：阶级对抗不可调和的产物

1. The State: A Product of the Irreconcilability of Class Antagonisms

如今马克思的理论所遭遇的，在历史上曾多次发生在为解放而奋斗的革命思想家和被压迫阶级领袖的理论身上。在伟大革命家的生前，压迫阶级不断地迫害他们，用最野蛮的恶意、最激烈的仇恨和最肆无忌惮的谎言和诽谤来攻击他们的理论。在他们去世后，压迫阶级试图将他们塑造成无害的偶像，将他们神化，并在一定程度上美化他们的名字，以此来“安慰”被压迫阶级，欺骗他们，同时剥夺革命理论的实质，削弱其革命锋芒，使其庸俗化。今天，资产阶级和工人运动中的机会主义者也参与了这种对马克思主义的篡改。他们忽略、掩盖或歪曲了这一理论的革命性一面，即其革命的灵魂。他们把资产阶级认可或看似认可的东西推到台前，大肆宣扬。所有社会沙文主义者现在都成了“马克思主义者”（别笑！）。而且，德国资产阶级学者——他们昨天还是马克思主义的歼灭专家——越来越频繁地谈论起“德国民族马克思”，他们声称，正是马克思培养了那些组织得如此精良、旨在发动掠夺性战争的工会！

What is now happening to Marx's theory has, in the course of history, happened repeatedly to the theories of revolutionary thinkers and leaders of oppressed classes fighting for emancipation. During the lifetime of great revolutionaries, the oppressing classes constantly hounded them, received their theories with the most savage malice, the most furious hatred and the most unscrupulous campaigns of lies and slander. After their death, attempts are made to convert them into harmless icons, to canonize them, so to say, and to hallow their names to a certain extent for the "consolation" of the oppressed classes and with the object of duping the latter, while at the same time robbing the revolutionary theory of its substance, blunting its revolutionary edge and vulgarizing it. Today, the bourgeoisie and the opportunists within the labor movement concur in this doctoring of Marxism. They omit, obscure, or distort the revolutionary side of this theory, its revolutionary soul. They push to the foreground and extol what is or seems acceptable to the bourgeoisie. All the social-chauvinists are now "Marxists" (don't laugh!). And more and more frequently German bourgeois scholars, only yesterday specialists in the annihilation of Marxism, are speaking of the "national-German" Marx, who, they claim, educated the labor unions which are so splendidly organized for the purpose of waging a predatory war!

鉴于马克思主义被前所未有地广泛歪曲，我们首要的任务是重新确立马克思关于国家问题的真正教义。这必然需要大量引用马克思和恩格斯的著作原文。当然，大量的引用会使文本冗长繁琐，不利于其普及，但我们不能省略这些引用。所有，或者至少是马克思和恩格斯著作中关于国家问题的最重要的段落，都必须尽可能完整地引用，以便读者能够对科学社会主义创始人的全部观点及其发展历程形成独立的认识，并能以文献资料证明和清晰地阐明当前盛行的“考茨基主义”对这些观点的歪曲。

In these circumstances, in view of the unprecedently wide-spread distortion of Marxism, our prime task is to re-establish what Marx really taught on the subject of the state. This will necessitate a number of long quotations from the works of Marx and Engels themselves. Of course, long quotations will render the text cumbersome and not help at all to make it popular reading, but we cannot possibly dispense with them. All, or at any rate all they most essential passages in the works of Marx and Engels on the subject of the state must by all means be quoted as fully as possible so that the reader may form an independent opinion of the totality of the views of the founders of scientific socialism, and of the evolution of those views, and so that their distortion by the "Kautskyism" now prevailing may be documentarily proved and clearly demonstrated.

让我们从恩格斯最受欢迎的著作《家庭、私有制和国家的起源》开始，该书第六版早在1894年就在斯图加特出版。我们必须翻译德文原文中的引文，因为俄文译本虽然数量众多，但大多不完整或非常不令人满意。

Let us being with the most popular of Engels' works, The Origin of the Family, Private Property and the State, the sixth edition of which was published in Stuttgart as far back as 1894. We have to translate the quotations from the German originals, as the Russian translations, while very numerous, are for the most part either incomplete or very unsatisfactory.

恩格斯总结他的历史分析时说：

Summing up his historical analysis, Engels says:

因此，国家绝非强加于社会的外部力量；也绝非如黑格尔所言的“伦理理念的现实”、“理性的形象和现实”。相反，它是社会在特定发展阶段的产物；它承认社会已陷入自身无法解决的矛盾之中，分裂成无法调和的对立面，而自身却无力消除这些对立。为了避免这些对立面，这些经济利益相互冲突的阶级，在徒劳的斗争中自我消耗并最终毁灭社会，就必须存在一种看似凌驾于社会之上的力量，以缓解冲突并将其维持在“秩序”的范围内；而这种源于社会却凌驾于社会之上，并日益疏离于社会的权力，便是国家。

"The state is, therefore, by no means a power forced on society from without; just as little is it 'the reality of the ethical idea', 'the image and reality of reason', as Hegel maintains. Rather, it is a product of society at a certain stage of development; it is the admission that this society has become entangled in an insoluble contradiction with itself, that it has split into irreconcilable antagonisms which it is powerless to dispel. But in order that these antagonisms, these classes with conflicting economic interests, might not consume themselves and society in fruitless struggle, it became necessary to have a power, seemingly standing above society, that would alleviate the conflict and keep it within the bounds of 'order'; and this power, arisen out of society but placing itself above it, and alienating itself more and more from it, is the state."

（第177-178页，第六版）

(pp.177-78, sixth edition)

这清晰地表达了马克思主义关于国家历史角色和意义的基本思想。国家是阶级对抗不可调和的产物和体现。当阶级对抗客观上无法调和时，国家便产生了。反之，国家的存在也证明了阶级对抗是不可调和的。

This expresses with perfect clarity the basic idea of Marxism with regard to the historical role and the meaning of the state. The state is a product and a manifestation of the irreconcilability of class antagonisms. The state arises where, when and insofar as class antagonism objectively cannot be reconciled. And, conversely, the existence of the state proves that the class antagonisms are irreconcilable.

正是从这个最重要、最根本的问题上，马克思主义的歪曲开始了，这种歪曲沿着两条主要路线发展。

It is on this most important and fundamental point that the distortion of Marxism, proceeding along two main lines, begins.

一方面，资产阶级，尤其是小资产阶级意识形态家，迫于无可辩驳的历史事实不得不承认，国家的存在恰恰是因为存在阶级对抗和阶级斗争。他们“修正”马克思，使之看起来像是阶级和解的工具。马克思认为，如果阶级能够和解，国家既不可能产生，也不可能维持。然而，从小资产阶级和庸俗的教授、评论家们频繁且善意地引用马克思的言论来看，国家似乎确实能够调和阶级。在马克思看来，国家是阶级统治的工具，是阶级压迫的工具；它是“秩序”的创造者，通过缓和阶级冲突来使这种压迫合法化并使其永久化。然而，在小资产阶级政治家看来，秩序意味着阶级的和解，而不是一个阶级对另一个阶级的压迫；缓解冲突意味着阶级的和解，而不是剥夺被压迫阶级推翻压迫者的明确手段和斗争方法。

On the one hand, the bourgeois, and particularly the petty-bourgeois, ideologists, compelled under the weight of indisputable historical facts to admit that the state only exists where there are class antagonisms and a class struggle, "correct" Marx in such a way as to make it appear that the gate is an organ for the reconciliation of classes. According to Marx, the state could neither have arisen nor maintained itself had it been possible to reconcile classes. From what the petty-bourgeois and philistine professors and publicists say, with quite frequent and benevolent references to Marx, it appears that the state does reconcile classes. According to Marx, the state is an organ of class rule, an organ for the oppression of one class by another; it is the creation of "order", which legalizes and perpetuates this oppression by moderating the conflict between classes. In the opinion of the petty-bourgeois politicians, however, order means the reconciliation of classes, and not the oppression of one class by another; to alleviate the conflict means reconciling classes and not depriving the oppressed classes of definite means and methods of struggle to overthrow the oppressors.

例如，在1917年革命中，当国家的重要性和作用问题作为一个需要立即采取行动，而且是大规模行动的实际问题，以其全部重要性凸显出来时，所有社会革命党人和孟什维克都立刻堕落到小资产阶级理论的窠臼，认为“国家”能够“调和”阶级。这两个政党的政治家们发表的无数决议和文章都充斥着这种小资产阶级的、庸俗的“调和”理论。小资产阶级民主人士永远无法理解，国家是某个特定阶级的统治工具，而这个阶级不可能与其对立阶级（即与它相对的阶级）相调和。他们对国家的态度最明显地表明，我们的社会革命党人和孟什维克根本不是社会主义者（这一点我们布尔什维克一直坚持），而是使用接近社会主义措辞的小资产阶级民主派。

For instance, when, in the revolution of 1917, the question of the significance and role of the state arose in all its magnitude as a practical question demanding immediate action, and, moreover, action on a mass scale, all the Social-Revolutionaries and Mensheviks descended at once to the petty-bourgeois theory that the "state" "reconciles" classes. Innumerable resolutions and articles by politicians of both these parties are thoroughly saturated with this petty-bourgeois and philistine "reconciliation" theory. That the state is an organ of the rule of a definite class which cannot be reconciled with its antipode (the class opposite to it) is something the petty-bourgeois democrats will never be able to understand. Their attitude to the state is one of the most striking manifestations of the fact that our Socialist- Revolutionaries and Mensheviks are not socialists at all (a point that we Bolsheviks have always maintained), but petty-bourgeois democrats using near-socialist phraseology.

另一方面，“考茨基式”对马克思主义的歪曲则更为隐蔽。“理论上”，国家是阶级统治的工具，阶级对抗是不可调和的，这一点并不否认。但被忽略或粉饰的是：如果国家是阶级对抗不可调和的产物，如果它是一种凌驾于社会之上并“日益与社会异化”的权力，那么显然，被压迫阶级的解放不仅离不开暴力革命，也离不开对统治阶级所建立的、正是这种“异化”体现的国家政权机器的摧毁。正如我们稍后将看到的，马克思基于对革命任务的具体历史分析，非常明确地得出了这一理论上不言自明的结论。而——正如我们将在后文详细阐述的——正是这一结论被考茨基“遗忘”并歪曲了。

On the other hand, the "Kautskyite" distortion of Marxism is far more subtle. "Theoretically", it is not denied that the state is an organ of class rule, or that class antagonisms are irreconcilable. But what is overlooked or glossed over is this: if the state is the product of the irreconcilability of class antagonisms, if it is a power standing above society and "alienating itself more and more from it", it is clear that the liberation of the oppressed class is impossible not only without a violent revolution, but also without the destruction of the apparatus of state power which was created by the ruling class and which is the embodiment of this "alienation". As we shall see later, Marx very explicitly drew this theoretically self-evident conclusion on the strength of a concrete historical analysis of the tasks of the revolution. And — as we shall show in detail further on — it is this conclusion which Kautsky has "forgotten" and distorted.



 



 

2. 武装人员特种部队、监狱等

2. Special Bodies of Armed Men, Prisons, etc.

恩格斯继续说道：

Engels continues:

“与旧的氏族（部落或氏族）秩序不同，国家首先是根据领土划分其臣民……”

"As distinct from the old gentile [tribal or clan] order, the state, first, divides its subjects according to territory...."

这种划分在我们看来似乎是“自然而然的”，但实际上却需要与旧有的世代或部落组织进行长期的斗争。

This division seems "natural" to us, but it costs a prolonged struggle against the old organization according to generations or tribes.

“第二个显著特征是公共权力的建立，这种权力不再直接与民众自发组织的武装力量相一致。这种特殊的公共权力是必要的，因为自从阶级分化以来，民众自发组织的武装力量已不可能存在……这种公共权力存在于每个国家；它不仅包括武装人员，还包括各种物质附属设施、监狱和强制机构，而这些是氏族社会所不了解的……”

"The second distinguishing feature is the establishment of a public power which no longer directly coincides with the population organizing itself as an armed force. This special, public power is necessary because a self-acting armed organization of the population has become impossible since the split into classes.... This public power exists in every state; it consists not merely of armed men but also of material adjuncts, prisons, and institutions of coercion of all kinds, of which gentile [clan] society knew nothing...."

恩格斯阐述了“权力”的概念，即所谓的国家权力。这种权力产生于社会，却凌驾于社会之上，并日益与社会疏离。这种权力主要由什么构成呢？它由拥有监狱等设施的特殊武装力量组成。

Engels elucidates the concept the concept of the "power" which is called the state, a power which arose from society but places itself above it and alienates itself more and more from it. What does this power mainly consist of? It consists of special bodies of armed men having prisons, etc., at their command.

我们有理由谈论武装人员的特殊团体，因为作为每个国家属性的公共权力“并不直接与”武装民众及其“自主行动的武装组织”相一致。

We are justified in speaking of special bodies of armed men, because the public power which is an attribute of every state "does not directly coincide" with the armed population, with its "self-acting armed organization".

像所有伟大的革命思想家一样，恩格斯试图让有阶级觉悟的工人注意到那些被当时盛行的庸俗主义视为最不值得关注、最习以为常、且被根深蒂固的偏见所奉为圭臬的事物。常备军和警察是国家权力的主要工具。但又怎能不是如此呢？

Like all great revolutionary thinkers, Engels tries to draw the attention of the class-conscious workers to what prevailing philistinism regards as least worthy of attention, as the most habitual thing, hallowed by prejudices that are not only deep-rooted but, one might say, petrified. A standing army and police are the chief instruments of state power. But how can it be otherwise?

对于恩格斯所面向的19世纪末的绝大多数欧洲人来说，由于他们既没有经历过也没有密切关注过任何一场伟大的革命，因此情况也只能如此。他们根本无法理解什么是“民众的自主武装组织”。当被问及为何需要将特殊的武装力量置于社会之上，使其与社会疏离（例如警察和常备军）时，这些西欧和俄国的庸俗之辈往往会引用斯宾塞或米哈伊洛夫斯基的几句名言，来解释社会生活的日益复杂化、职能的分化等等。

From the viewpoint of the vast majority of Europeans of the end of the 19th century, whom Engels was addressing, and who had not gone through or closely observed a single great revolution, it could not have been otherwise. They could not understand at all what a "self-acting armed organization of the population" was. When asked why it became necessary to have special bodies of armed men placed above society and alienating themselves from it (police and a standing army), the West-European and Russian philistines are inclined to utter a few phrases borrowed from Spencer of Mikhailovsky, to refer to the growing complexity of social life, the differentiation of functions, and so on.

这种说法看似“科学”，实际上却掩盖了一个重要而基本的事实，即社会分裂成不可调和的对立阶级，从而有效地使普通人昏昏欲睡。

Such a reference seems "scientific", and effectively lulls the ordinary person to sleep by obscuring the important and basic fact, namely, the split of society into irreconcilable antagonistic classes.

如果没有这种分裂，“民众的自主武装组织”与手持棍棒的原始猴群、原始人或部落形式的原始人组织相比，其复杂性、技术水平等等都会有所不同。但这样的组织仍然是可能的。

Were it not for this split, the "self-acting armed organization of the population" would differ from the primitive organization of a stick-wielding herd of monkeys, or of primitive men, or of men united in clans, by its complexity, its high technical level, and so on. But such an organization would still be possible.

这是不可能的，因为文明社会分裂成相互对立、而且是不可调和的对立阶级，这些阶级的“自我武装”只会导致彼此之间的武装斗争。国家兴起，特殊权力产生，特殊的武装力量出现，每一次革命，通过摧毁国家机器，都向我们揭示了赤裸裸的阶级斗争，清楚地表明了统治阶级如何竭力重建为其服务的武装力量，以及被压迫阶级如何竭力建立一种新的、能够为被剥削者而非剥削者服务的武装组织。

It is impossible because civilized society is split into antagonistic, and, moreover, irreconcilably antagonistic classes, whose "self-acting" arming would lead to an armed struggle between them. A state arises, a special power is created, special bodies of armed men, and every revolution, by destroying the state apparatus, shows us the naked class struggle, clearly shows us how the ruling class strives to restore the special bodies of armed men which serve it, and how the oppressed class strives to create a new organization of this kind, capable of serving the exploited instead of the exploiters.

在上述论证中，恩格斯从理论上提出了与每一次伟大革命在实践中都向我们提出的同一个问题，这个问题既切实可感，又具有群众运动的规模，那就是“特殊”武装力量与“人民的自主武装组织”之间的关系问题。我们将看到，欧洲革命和俄国革命的经验是如何具体地阐释这个问题的。

In the above argument, Engels raises theoretically the very same question which every great revolution raises before us in practice, palpably and, what is more, on a scale of mass action, namely, the question of the relationship between "special" bodies of armed men and the "self-acting armed organization of the population". We shall see how this question is specifically illustrated by the experience of the European and Russian revolutions.

但让我们回到恩格尔的阐述。

But to return to Engel's exposition.

他指出，有时——例如在北美某些地区——这种公共权力很弱（他指的是资本主义社会中一个罕见的例外，以及北美帝国主义之前的自由殖民者占主导地位的地区），但总的来说，它会变得越来越强：

He points out that sometimes — in certain parts of North America, for example — this public power is weak (he has in mind a rare exception in capitalist society, and those parts of North America in its pre-imperialist days where the free colonists predominated), but that, generally speaking, it grows stronger:

“然而，随着国家内部阶级对抗的加剧，以及邻近国家面积和人口的增长，公共权力也会相应增强。我们只需看看当今的欧洲，那里阶级斗争和征服竞争已经将公共权力推向了如此高的程度，以至于它有吞噬整个社会乃至国家的危险。”

"It [the public power] grows stronger, however, in proportion as class antagonisms within the state become more acute, and as adjacent states become larger and more populous. We have only to look at our present-day Europe, where class struggle and rivalry in conquest have tuned up the public power to such a pitch that it threatens to swallow the whole of society and even the state."

这段文字写于上世纪九十年代初，恩格尔的最后一篇序言日期为1891年6月16日。当时，转向帝国主义——意味着托拉斯的完全统治、大银行的无所不能、大规模的殖民政策等等——在法国才刚刚起步，在北美和德国则更为微弱。自那时起，“征服竞争”便突飞猛进，尤其是在20世纪第二个十年之初，世界已被这些“征服竞争者”，也就是掠夺成性的列强瓜分殆尽。此后，军事和海军军备呈爆炸式增长，1914-1917年英国或德国为争夺世界霸权、瓜分战利品而发动的掠夺性战争，几乎将社会所有力量都吞噬殆尽，使之濒临彻底的灾难。

This was written not later than the early nineties of the last century, Engel's last preface being dated June 16, 1891. The turn towards imperialism — meaning the complete domination of the trusts, the omnipotence of the big banks, a grand-scale colonial policy, and so forth — was only just beginning in France, and was even weaker in North America and in Germany. Since then "rivalry in conquest" has taken a gigantic stride, all the more because by the beginning of the second decade of the 20th century the world had been completely divided up among these "rivals in conquest", i.e., among the predatory Great Powers. Since then, military and naval armaments have grown fantastically and the predatory war of 1914-17 for the domination of the world by Britain or Germany, for the division of the spoils, has brought the "swallowing" of all the forces of society by the rapacious state power close to complete catastrophe.

早在1891年，恩格斯就指出“征服的竞争”是列强外交政策最重要的特征之一，而自1914年以来，社会沙文主义的无赖们，在这种竞争多次加剧并引发帝国主义战争之后，就一直用“保卫祖国”、“保卫共和国和革命”等口号来掩盖他们“自己”资产阶级掠夺性利益的捍卫！

Engels' could, as early as 1891, point to "rivalry in conquest" as one of the most important distinguishing features of the foreign policy of the Great Powers, while the social-chauvinist scoundrels have ever since 1914, when this rivalry, many time intensified, gave rise to an imperialist war, been covering up the defence of the predatory interests of "their own" bourgeoisie with phrases about "defence of the fatherland", "defence of the republic and the revolution", etc.!



 



 

3. 国家：剥削被压迫阶级的工具

3. The State: an Instrument for the Exploitation of the Oppressed Class

维持凌驾于社会之上的特殊公共权力需要税收和国家贷款。

The maintenance of the special public power standing above society requires taxes and state loans.

恩格斯写道：“官员们掌握了公共权力和征税权，如今作为社会机关，凌驾于社会之上。即使他们能够获得那种自由、自愿给予氏族宪法机关的尊重，也无法满足他们……”于是，专门制定法律来宣扬官员的神圣性和豁免权。“最卑微的警察”都比氏族代表拥有更大的“权威”，但即使是文明国家的军事首脑，也可能羡慕氏族长老所享有的“不受约束的社会尊重”。

"Having pubic power and the right to levy taxes," Engels writes, "the officials now stand, as organs of society, above society. The free, voluntary respect that was accorded to the organs of the gentile [clan] constitution does not satisfy them, even if they could gain it...." Special laws are enacted proclaiming the sanctity and immunity of the officials. "The shabbiest police servant" has more "authority" than the representative of the clan, but even the head of the military power of a civilized state may well envy the elder of a clan the "unrestrained respect" of society.

这里提出了官员作为国家权力机关的特权地位问题。其核心问题是：是什么使他们凌驾于社会之上？我们将看到，1871年的巴黎公社是如何在实践中回答这一理论问题的，以及考茨基在1912年是如何从反动立场上掩盖这一问题的。

The question of the privileged position of the officials as organs of state power is raised here. The main point indicated is: what is it that places them above society? We shall see how this theoretical question was answered in practice by the Paris Commune in 1871 and how it was obscured from a reactionary standpoint by kautsky in 1912.

“由于国家是为了遏制阶级对抗而产生的，但同时又诞生于这些阶级的冲突之中，因此，它通常是经济上最强大的统治阶级的国家，而这个阶级又通过国家这一媒介，成为政治上的统治阶级，从而获得压制和剥削被压迫阶级的新手段……”古代和封建国家是剥削奴隶和农奴的工具；同样，“现代代议制国家也是资本剥削雇佣劳动的工具。然而，也有例外，在某些时期，交战的阶级势均力敌，以至于作为表面上的调解者的国家权力，暂时获得了某种程度的独立于双方的力量……”17世纪和18世纪的绝对君主制国家、法国第一帝国和第二帝国的波拿巴主义政权以及德国的俾斯麦政权，都属于这种情况。

"Because the state arose from the need to hold class antagonisms in check, but because it arose, at the same time, in the midst of the conflict of these classes, it is, as a rule, the state of the most powerful, economically dominant class, which, through the medium of the state, becomes also the politically dominant class, and thus acquires new means of holding down and exploiting the oppressed class...." The ancient and feudal states were organs for the exploitation of the slaves and serfs; likewise, "the modern representative state is an instrument of exploitation of wage-labor by capital. By way of exception, however, periods occur in which the warring classes balance each other so nearly that the state power as ostensible mediator acquires, for the moment, a certain degree of independence of both...." Such were the absolute monarchies of the 17th and 18th centuries, the Bonapartism of the First and Second Empires in France, and the Bismarck regime in Germany.

我们还可以补充一点，这就是克伦斯基政府在俄国共和国时期开始迫害革命无产阶级以来的情形。当时，由于小资产阶级民主派的领导，苏维埃已经变得无能为力，而资产阶级还不够强大，无法简单地驱散他们。

Such, we may add, is the Kerensky government in republican Russia since it began to persecute the revolutionary proletariat, at a moment when, owing to the leadership of the petty-bourgeois democrats, the Soviets have already become impotent, while the bourgeoisie are not yet strong enough simply to disperse them.

恩格斯继续说道，在一个民主共和国里，“财富间接地、但却更加可靠地行使权力”，首先是通过“直接腐败官员”（美国）；其次是通过“政府与证券交易所的联盟”（法国和美国）。

In a democratic republic, Engels continues, "wealth exercises its power indirectly, but all the more surely", first, by means of the "direct corruption of officials" (America); secondly, by means of an "alliance of the government and the Stock Exchange" (France and America).

目前，帝国主义和银行的控制已经将维护和实现财富在各种民主共和国中无所不能的这两种手段“发展”成了一种特殊的艺术。例如，在俄罗斯民主共和国成立之初的几个月里，可以说正值“社会主义”的社会革命党人和孟什维克与资产阶级在联合政府中结成“婚姻”的蜜月期，帕尔钦斯基先生阻挠了所有旨在遏制资本家及其掠夺行为、通过战争合同掠夺国家财产的措施；后来，帕尔钦斯基先生辞去内阁职务（当然，他的继任者是另一个与他如出一辙的帕尔钦斯基），却被资本家“奖励”了一份年薪12万卢布的高薪工作——你会如何称呼这种行为？直接贿赂还是间接贿赂？是政府与集团的勾结，还是“仅仅”是友好关系？切尔诺夫家族、采列捷利家族、阿夫克森季耶夫家族和斯科别列夫家族扮演着什么角色？他们是百万富翁国库掠夺者的“直接”盟友，还是仅仅是间接盟友？

At present, imperialism and the domination of the banks have "developed" into an exceptional art both these methods of upholding and giving effect to the omnipotence of wealth in democratic republics of all descriptions. Since, for instance, in the very first months of the Russian democratic republic, one might say during the honeymoon of the "socialist" S.R.s and Mensheviks joined in wedlock to the bourgeoisie, in the coalition government. Mr. Palchinsky obstructed every measure intended for curbing the capitalists and their marauding practices, their plundering of the state by means of war contracts; and since later on Mr. Palchinsky, upon resigning from the Cabinet (and being, of course, replaced by another quite similar Palchinsky), was "rewarded" by the capitalists with a lucrative job with a salary of 120,000 rubles per annum — what would you call that? Direct or indirect bribery? An alliance of the government and the syndicates, or "merely" friendly relations? What role do the Chernovs, Tseretelis, Avksentyevs and Skobelevs play? Are they the "direct" or only the indirect allies of the millionaire treasury-looters?

在民主共和国中，“财富”的至高无上性更加确凿的另一个原因是，它并不依赖于政治机器的缺陷或资本主义有缺陷的政治外壳。民主共和国是资本主义所能拥有的最佳政治外壳，因此，一旦资本（通过帕尔钦斯基、切尔诺夫、采列捷利等人）掌控了这个最佳外壳，它就能如此稳固地确立自己的权力，以至于资产阶级民主共和国中任何人、机构或政党的更迭都无法动摇它。

Another reason why the omnipotence of "wealth" is more certain in a democratic republic is that it does not depend on defects in the political machinery or on the faulty political shell of capitalism. A democratic republic is the best possible political shell for capitalism, and, therefore, once capital has gained possession of this very best shell (through the Palchinskys, Chernovs, Tseretelis and Co.), it establishes its power so securely, so firmly, that no change of persons, institutions or parties in the bourgeois-democratic republic can shake it.

我们还必须注意到，恩格斯非常明确地指出，普选权也是资产阶级统治的工具。他显然是考虑到德国社会民主党的长期经验，指出普选权是……

We must also note that Engels is most explicit in calling universal suffrage as well an instrument of bourgeois rule. Universal suffrage, he says, obviously taking account of the long experience of German Social-Democracy, is

“这是衡量工人阶级成熟度的标尺。在当今社会，它不可能也不可能具有其他任何意义。”

"the gauge of the maturity of the working class. It cannot and never will be anything more in the present-day state."

像我们的社会革命党人和孟什维克这样的小资产阶级民主派，以及他们的孪生兄弟——西欧所有的社会沙文主义者和机会主义者——都期望从普选中获得“更多”。他们自己也持有这种错误的观念，并向人民灌输这种观念，即“在当今国家”，普选真的能够反映大多数劳动人民的意愿并确保其实现。

The petty-bourgeois democrats, such as our Socialist-Revolutionaries and Mensheviks, and also their twin brothers, all the social-chauvinists and opportunists of Western Europe, expect just this "more" from universal suffrage. They themselves share, and instil into the minds of the people, the false notion that universal suffrage "in the present-day state" is really capable of revealing the will of the majority of the working people and of securing its realization.

在此，我们只能指出这种错误观念，只能指出恩格斯清晰明确的论述在“官方”（即机会主义的）社会主义政党的宣传鼓动中处处遭到歪曲。关于恩格斯在此轻描淡写的这种观念的彻底谬误，我们将在后续论述马克思和恩格斯关于“现代”国家的观点时进行详细揭露。

Here, we can only indicate this false notion, only point out that Engels' perfectly clear statement is distorted at every step in the propaganda and agitation of the "official" (i.e., opportunist) socialist parties. A detailed exposure of the utter falsity of this notion which engels brushes aside here is given in our further account of the views of Marx and Engels on the "present-day" state.

恩格斯在其最受欢迎的著作中用以下这段话概括了他的观点：

Engels gives a general summary of his views in the most popular of his works in the following words:

“因此，国家并非自古有之。历史上也存在过没有国家的社会，它们对国家和国家权力一无所知。在经济发展的某个阶段，由于社会阶级的分裂，国家才成为一种必然。如今，我们正迅速接近生产发展的另一个阶段，届时，这些阶级的存在不仅不再是必需的，反而会成为生产的阻碍。它们将像在早期阶段兴起时一样走向衰落。随之而来的，是国家必然的衰落。届时，社会将以生产者自由平等的联合为基础重组生产，并将整个国家机器安置在它应有的位置：一座古董博物馆，与纺车和青铜斧为伴。”

"The state, then, has not existed from all eternity. There have been societies that did without it, that had no idea of the state and state power. At a certain stage of economic development, which was necessarily bound up with the split of society into classes, the state became a necessity owing to this split. We are now rapidly approaching a stage in the development of production at which the existence of these classes not only will have ceased to be a necessity, but will become a positive hindrance to production. They will fall as they arose at an earlier stage. Along with them the state will inevitably fall. Society, which will reorganize production on the basis of a free and equal association of the producers, will put the whole machinery of state where it will then belong: into a museum of antiquities, by the side of the spinning-wheel and the bronze axe."

在当今社会民主党的宣传鼓动文献中，我们很少见到这段话。即便偶尔见到，引用也大多如同膜拜圣像一般，仅仅是为了表达对恩格斯的官方敬意，而丝毫没有尝试去理解这种将“整个国家机器贬为古董博物馆”的做法所蕴含的革命的广度和深度。在大多数情况下，我们甚至都找不到对恩格斯所说的“国家机器”的理解。

We do not often come across this passage in the propaganda and agitation literature of the present-day Social-Democrats. Even when we do come across it, it is mostly quoted in the same manner as one bows before an icon, i.e., it is done to show official respect for Engels, and no attempt is made to gauge the breadth and depth of the revolution that this relegating of "the whole machinery of state to a museum of antiquities" implies. In most cases we do not even find an understanding of what Engels calls the state machine.







 







 

4. 国家的“衰落”与暴力革命

4. The "Withering Away" of the State, and Violent Revolution

恩格斯关于国家“消亡”的论述广为人知，常被引用，并且如此清晰地揭示了马克思主义惯常地迎合机会主义的本质，因此我们必须详细论述。我们将引用其全部论证。

Engel's words regarding the "withering away" of the state are so widely known, they are often quoted, and so clearly reveal the essence of the customary adaptation of Marxism to opportunism that we must deal with them in detail. We shall quote the whole argument from which they are taken.

“无产阶级首先夺取国家政权，将生产资料收归国有。但在此过程中，它消灭了自身作为无产阶级的存在，消灭了一切阶级区别和阶级对抗，也消灭了国家本身。此前，社会在阶级对抗中运作，需要国家，即特定剥削阶级的组织，来维持其外部生产条件，因此，尤其需要国家来强制被剥削阶级继续处于既定生产方式（奴隶制、农奴制或奴役制、雇佣劳动）所决定的压迫条件下。国家是整个社会的官方代表，是社会在一个可见的团体中的集中体现。但这仅仅是因为它是代表其时代整个社会的阶级的国家：在古代，是奴隶主阶级的国家；在中世纪，是封建贵族阶级的国家；在我们这个时代，是资产阶级的国家。”当国家最终成为整个社会的真正代表时，它自身便变得不再必要。一旦不再有任何社会阶级需要被统治，一旦阶级统治，以及基于当前生产无政府状态的个人生存斗争，连同由此斗争产生的冲突和过激行为，都被消除，就再也没有什么东西需要被统治——没有什么需要特殊的强制力量，即国家。国家真正作为整个社会的代表而出现的第一个行动——以社会的名义占有生产资料——也是它作为国家最后的独立行动。国家对社会关系的干预在各个领域都变得多余，然后自然消亡。对人的统治被对物的管理和对生产过程的引导所取代。国家并非“废除”，而是逐渐消亡。这体现了“自由人民的国家”这一短语的价值，无论从其长期以来在煽动性立场上的合理使用来看，还是从其在社会发展中的作用来看，都是如此。观点，以及其最终的科学不足；还有所谓无政府主义者要求一夜之间废除国家的要求。

"The proletariat seizes from state power and turns the means of production into state property to begin with. But thereby it abolishes itself as the proletariat, abolishes all class distinctions and class antagonisms, and abolishes also the state as state. Society thus far, operating amid class antagonisms, needed the state, that is, an organization of the particular exploiting class, for the maintenance of its external conditions of production, and, therefore, especially, for the purpose of forcibly keeping the exploited class in the conditions of oppression determined by the given mode of production (slavery, serfdom or bondage, wage-labor). The state was the official representative of society as a whole, its concentration in a visible corporation. But it was this only insofar as it was the state of that class which itself represented, for its own time, society as a whole: in ancient times, the state of slave-owning citizens; in the Middle Ages, of the feudal nobility; in our own time, of the bourgeoisie. When at last it becomes the real representative of the whole of society, it renders itself unnecessary. As soon as there is no longer any social class to be held in subjection, as soon as class rule, and the individual struggle for existence based upon the present anarchy in production, with the collisions and excesses arising from this struggle, are removed, nothing more remains to be held in subjection — nothing necessitating a special coercive force, a state. The first act by which the state really comes forward as the representative of the whole of society — the taking possession of the means of production in the name of society — is also its last independent act as a state. State interference in social relations becomes, in one domain after another, superfluous, and then dies down of itself. The government of persons is replaced by the administration of things, and by the conduct of processes of production. The state is not 'abolished'. It withers away. This gives the measure of the value of the phrase 'a free people's state', both as to its justifiable use for a long time from an agitational point of view, and as to its ultimate scientific insufficiency; and also of the so-called anarchists' demand that the state be abolished overnight."

（《尤金·杜林先生的科学革命》（反杜林），

第301-303页，德文第三版。）

(Herr Eugen Duhring's Revolution in Science [Anti-Duhring],

pp.301-03, third German edition.)

可以肯定地说，恩格斯这一论证思想极其丰富，但现代社会主义政党中只有一点真正融入了社会主义思想，那就是马克思认为国家会“消亡”——这与无政府主义“废除”国家的理论截然不同。如此大幅度地删减马克思主义，无异于将其贬低为机会主义，因为这种“解释”只留下一个模糊的概念，即缓慢、均匀、渐进地改变，没有飞跃和风暴，没有革命。当前这种广泛流传的、流行（如果可以这么说的话）的关于国家“消亡”的观念，无疑是在掩盖革命，甚至否定革命。

It is safe to say that of this argument of Engels', which is so remarkably rich in ideas, only one point has become an integral part of socialist thought among modern socialist parties, namely, that according to Marx that state "withers away" — as distinct from the anarchist doctrine of the "abolition" of the state. To prune Marxism to such an extent means reducing it to opportunism, for this "interpretation" only leaves a vague notion of a slow, even, gradual change, of absence of leaps and storms, of absence of revolution. The current, widespread, popular, if one may say so, conception of the "withering away" of the state undoubtedly means obscuring, if not repudiating, revolution.

然而，这种“解释”是对马克思主义最粗暴的歪曲，只对资产阶级有利。在理论层面上，它无视了恩格斯刚才全文引述的“总结性”论证中指出的最重要的情况和考虑因素。

Such an "interpretation", however, is the crudest distortion of Marxism, advantageous only to the bourgeoisie. In point of theory, it is based on disregard for the most important circumstances and considerations indicated in, say, Engels' "summary" argument we have just quoted in full.

首先，恩格斯在其论证之初便指出，无产阶级通过夺取国家政权，“废除了作为国家的政权”。我们无需深究其含义。通常，人们要么完全忽略这句话，要么将其视为恩格斯某种“黑格尔式的弱点”。然而，事实上，这些话简明扼要地表达了最伟大的无产阶级革命之一——1871年巴黎公社的经验，我们将在适当的地方对此进行更详细的论述。事实上，恩格斯在此所说的是无产阶级革命“废除”了资产阶级国家，而关于国家消亡的说法指的是社会主义革命后无产阶级国家的残余。在恩格斯看来，资产阶级国家并非“消亡”，而是在革命过程中被无产阶级“废除”。这场革命之后消亡的，是无产阶级国家或半国家。

In the first place, at the very outset of his argument, Engels says that, in seizing state power, the proletariat thereby "abolishes the state as state". It is not done to ponder over over the meaning of this. Generally, it is either ignored altogether, or is considered to be something in the nature of "Hegelian weakness" on Engels' part. As a matter of fact, however, these words briefly express the experience of one of the greatest proletarian revolutions, the Paris Commune of 1871, of which we shall speak in greater detail in its proper place. As a matter of fact, Engels speaks here of the proletariat revolution "abolishing" the bourgeois state, while the words about the state withering away refer to the remnants of the proletarian state after the socialist revolution. According to Engels, the bourgeois state does not "wither away", but is "abolished" by the proletariat in the course of the revolution. What withers away after this revolution is the proletarian state or semi-state.

其次，国家是一种“特殊强制力”。恩格斯在此以极其清晰的方式给出了这个精彩而深刻的定义。由此可知，资产阶级镇压无产阶级、少数富人镇压数百万劳动人民的“特殊强制力”，必须被无产阶级镇压资产阶级的“特殊强制力”（无产阶级专政）所取代。这正是“废除国家作为国家”的含义。这正是以社会的名义占有生产资料的“行为”。显而易见，这种用一种（资产阶级的）“特殊强制力”取代另一种（无产阶级的）“特殊强制力”，绝不可能以“逐渐消亡”的方式发生。

Secondly, the state is a "special coercive force". Engels gives this splendid and extremely profound definition here with the utmost lucidity. And from it follows that the "special coercive force" for the suppression of the proletariat by the bourgeoisie, of millions of working people by handfuls of the rich, must be replaced by a "special coercive force" for the suppression of the bourgeoisie by the proletariat (the dictatorship of the proletariat). This is precisely what is meant by "abolition of the state as state". This is precisely the "act" of taking possession of the means of production in the name of society. And it is self-evident that such a replacement of one (bourgeois) "special force" by another (proletarian) "special force" cannot possibly take place in the form of "withering away".

第三，恩格斯在谈到国家“消亡”，以及更为形象生动的“自我消亡”时，非常明确地指的是“国家以全社会的名义占有生产资料”之后的时期，也就是社会主义革命之后的时期。我们都知道，那时“国家”的政治形式是最彻底的民主制。但是，那些厚颜无耻地歪曲马克思主义的机会主义者，却从未想到恩格斯在这里实际上是在谈论民主“自我消亡”或“消亡”。这乍一看似乎很奇怪。但只有那些没有思考过民主也是一种国家，因而当国家消失时民主也会消失的人，才会觉得这“难以理解”。只有革命才能“废除”资产阶级国家。国家本身，也就是最彻底的民主制，只能“消亡”。

Thirdly, in speaking of the state "withering away", and the even more graphic and colorful "dying down of itself", Engels refers quite clearly and definitely to the period after "the state has taken possession of the means of production in the name of the whole of society", that is, after the socialist revolution. We all know that the political form of the "state" at that time is the most complete democracy. But it never enters the head of any of the opportunists, who shamelessly distort Marxism, that Engels is consequently speaking here of democracy "dying down of itself", or "withering away". This seems very strange at first sight. But is is "incomprehensible" only to those who have not thought about democracy also being a state and, consequently, also disappearing when the state disappears. Revolution alone can "abolish" the bourgeois state. The state in general, i.e., the most complete democracy, can only "wither away".

第四，恩格斯在提出他著名的“国家消亡”论断之后，立即明确指出这一论断既针对机会主义者，也针对无政府主义者。在此过程中，恩格斯着重强调了从“国家消亡”论断中得出的、针对机会主义者的结论。

Fourthly, after formulating his famous proposition that "the state withers away", Engels at once explains specifically that this proposition is directed against both the opportunists and the anarchists. In doing this, Engels puts in the forefront that conclusion, drawn from the proposition that "the state withers away", which is directed against the opportunists.

可以打赌，在每10000个读过或听过“国家消亡”论的人中，有9990人完全不知道，或者根本不记得恩格斯得出这一结论并非仅仅针对无政府主义者。而剩下的10人中，可能有9人根本不知道“自由人民国家”的含义，也不明白为什么攻击这一口号就等同于攻击机会主义者。历史就是这样被书写的！伟大的革命理论就这样在不知不觉中被歪曲，并被迎合了当时盛行的庸俗主义。针对无政府主义者的结论被重复了成千上万遍，被庸俗化，以最肤浅的方式强加于人心，并逐渐演变成一种根深蒂固的偏见，而针对机会主义者的结论却被掩盖和“遗忘”了！

One can wager that out of every 10,000 persons who have read or heard about the "withering away" of the state, 9,990 are completely unaware, or do not remember, that Engels directed his conclusions from that proposition not against anarchists alone. And of the remaining 10, probably nine do not know the meaning of a "free people's state" or why an attack on this slogan means an attack on opportunists. This is how history is written! This is how a great revolutionary teaching is imperceptibly falsified and adapted to prevailing philistinism. The conclusion directed against the anarchists has been repeated thousands of times; it has been vulgarized, and rammed into people's heads in the shallowest form, and has acquired the strength of a prejudice, whereas the conclusion directed against the opportunists has been obscured and "forgotten"!

“自由人民国家”是七十年代德国社会民主党的一项纲领性要求和流行语。这个口号除了以一种浮夸庸俗的方式描述民主概念之外，没有任何政治内涵。恩格斯从鼓动的角度出发，准备“暂时”为使用这个词辩护，因为它在法律上允许地暗示了一种民主共和国。但这终究是一个机会主义的口号，因为它不仅仅是美化资产阶级民主，更是对社会主义对国家整体批判的无知。我们赞成民主共和国，认为它是资本主义下无产阶级的最佳国家形式。但我们也不能忘记，即使在最民主的资产阶级共和国里，人民仍然遭受着雇佣奴役。此外，每个国家都是镇压被压迫阶级的“特种部队”。因此，并非每个国家都是“自由的”或“人民的国家”。马克思和恩格斯在七十年代反复向他们的党内同志解释了这一点。

The "free people's state" was a programme demand and a catchword current among the German Social-Democrats in the seventies. this catchword is devoid of all political content except that it describes the concept of democracy in a pompous philistine fashion. Insofar as it hinted in a legally permissible manner at a democratic republic, Engels was prepared to "justify" its use "for a time" from an agitational point of view. But it was an opportunist catchword, for it amounted to something more than prettifying bourgeois democracy, and was also failure to understand the socialist criticism of the state in general. We are in favor of a democratic republic as the best form of state for the proletariat under capitalism. But we have no right to forget that wage slavery is the lot of the people even in the most democratic bourgeois republic. Furthermore, every state is a "special force" for the suppression of the oppressed class. Consequently, every state is not "free and not a "people's state". Marx and Engels explained this repeatedly to their party comrades in the seventies.

第五，恩格斯关于国家消亡的论述人尽皆知，而他同一部著作中也包含了关于暴力革命意义的论证。恩格斯对暴力革命作用的历史分析，实际上成了对暴力革命的颂扬。然而，这一点却“无人记得”。现代社会主义政党既不谈论也不思考这一思想的意义，它在他们的日常宣传鼓动工作中也完全不起作用。然而，它与国家的“消亡”密不可分，构成了一个和谐的整体。

Fifthly, the same work of Engels', whose arguments about the withering away of the state everyone remembers, also contains an argument of the significance of violent revolution. Engels' historical analysis of its role becomes a veritable panegyric on violent revolution. This, "no one remembers". It is not done in modern socialist parties to talk or even think about the significance of this idea, and it plays no part whatever in their daily propaganda and agitation among the people. And yet it is inseparably bound up with the 'withering away" of the state into one harmonious whole.

以下是恩格斯的论证：

Here is Engels' argument:

“……然而，这种力量在历史上还扮演着另一种角色（除了邪恶力量之外），那就是革命角色；用马克思的话来说，它是孕育新社会的旧社会的助产士，是社会运动冲破并粉碎死气沉沉、僵化僵化的政治形式的工具——杜林先生对此只字未提。他只是叹息着承认，或许为了推翻建立在剥削基础上的经济，武力是必要的——不幸的是，他认为，任何武力的使用都会使使用者自身丧失道德。而这发生在德国，一场暴力冲突——毕竟，这场冲突或许会被强加于人民——至少能够消除三十年战争屈辱之后渗透到德国民族精神中的奴性。而这个人的思维方式——迟钝、乏味、无能——竟然妄图强加于最革命的政党。”历史从未如此辉煌！

"...That force, however, plays yet another role [other than that of a diabolical power] in history, a revolutionary role; that, in the words of Marx, it is the midwife of every old society which is pregnant with a new one, that it is the instrument with which social movement forces its way through and shatters the dead, fossilized political forms — of this there is not a word in Herr Duhring. It is only with sighs and groans that he admits the possibility that force will perhaps be necessary for the overthrow of an economy based on exploitation — unfortunately, because all use of force demoralizes, he says, the person who uses it. And this in Germany, where a violent collision — which may, after all, be forced on the people — would at least have the advantage of wiping out the servility which has penetrated the nation's mentality following the humiliation of the Thirty Years' War. And this person's mode of thought — dull, insipid, and impotent — presumes to impose itself on the most revolutionary party that history has ever known!

（第193页，德文第三版，第二部分，第四章末尾）

(p.193, third German edition, Part II, end of Chap.IV)

恩格斯在 1878 年至 1894 年间，也就是直到他去世前，一直坚持向德国社会民主党人宣传暴力革命的这种赞美之词，如何能与国家“消亡”的理论结合起来，形成一个统一的理论呢？

How can this panegyric on violent revolution, which Engels insistently brought to the attention of the German Social-Democrats between 1878 and 1894, i.e., right up to the time of his death, be combined with the theory of the 'withering away" of the state to form a single theory?

通常，这两者是通过折衷主义结合起来的，即不加原则或诡辩地随意选择（或为了取悦当权者）先选择一个论点，然后再选择另一个论点。在99%的情况下，甚至更多，被置于首位的都是“衰败”的概念。辩证法被折衷主义所取代——这是当今官方社会民主党文献中关于马克思主义最常见、最普遍的做法。当然，这种替代并非新鲜事；早在古希腊哲学史上就已出现。以机会主义的方式歪曲马克思主义，用折衷主义取代辩证法，是欺骗民众最便捷的手段。它给人一种虚假的满足感；它似乎考虑到了过程的各个方面、所有发展趋势、所有相互冲突的影响等等，而实际上它根本没有提供任何关于社会发展过程的全面和革命性的概念。

Usually the two are combined by means of eclecticism, by an unprincipled or sophistic selection made arbitrarily (or to please the powers that be) of first one, then another argument, and in 99 cases out of 100, if not more, it is the idea of the "withering away" that is placed in the forefront. Dialectics are replaced by eclecticism — this is the most usual, the most wide-spread practice to be met with in present-day official Social-Democratic literature in relation to Marxism. This sort of substitution is, of course, nothing new; it was observed even in the history of classical Greek philosophy. In falsifying Marxism in opportunist fashion, the substitution of eclecticism for dialectics is the easiest way of deceiving the people. It gives an illusory satisfaction; it seems to take into account all sides of the process, all trends of development, all the conflicting influences, and so forth, whereas in reality it provides no integral and revolutionary conception of the process of social development at all.

前面我们已经说过，以后还会更充分地证明，马克思和恩格斯关于暴力革命不可避免的理论指的是资产阶级国家。后者不能通过无产阶级国家（无产阶级专政）的“自然消亡”过程而被取代，而通常只能通过暴力革命来实现。恩格斯对此的颂扬，与马克思的反复论述完全吻合（参见《哲学的贫困》和《共产党宣言》的结尾段落，其中骄傲而公开地宣告了暴力革命的必然性；参见马克思近30年后在批判1875年哥达纲领时所写的，他毫不留情地抨击了该纲领的机会主义性质）——这种颂扬绝非仅仅是“冲动”、仅仅是慷慨激昂的演说或仅仅是一场论战。系统地向群众灌输这种暴力革命观的必要性，正是马克思和恩格斯整个理论的根基。如今盛行的……背叛了他们的理论。社会沙文主义和考茨基主义倾向在这两种倾向中都有着显著的表现，它们无视此类宣传和煽动。

We have already said above, and shall show more fully later, that the theory of Marx and Engels of the inevitability of a violent revolution refers to the bourgeois state. The latter cannot be superseded by the proletarian state (the dictatorship of the proletariat) through the process of 'withering away", but, as a general rule, only through a violent revolution. The panegyric Engels sang in its honor, and which fully corresponds to Marx's repeated statements (see the concluding passages of The Poverty of Philosophy and the Communist Manifesto, with their proud and open proclamation of the inevitability of a violent revolution; see what Marx wrote nearly 30 years later, in criticizing the Gotha Programme of 1875, when he mercilessly castigated the opportunist character of that programme) — this panegyric is by no means a mere "impulse", a mere declamation or a polemical sally. The necessity of systematically imbuing the masses with this and precisely this view of violent revolution lies at the root of the entire theory of Marx and Engels. The betrayal of their theory by the now prevailing social-chauvinist and Kautskyite trends expresses itself strikingly in both these trends ignoring such propaganda and agitation.

没有暴力革命，资产阶级国家不可能被无产阶级国家所取代。无产阶级国家，也就是整个国家的废除，除了通过“自我消亡”的过程之外，是不可能的。

The supersession of the bourgeois state by the proletarian state is impossible without a violent revolution. The abolition of the proletarian state, i.e., of the state in general, is impossible except through the process of "withering away".

马克思和恩格斯在研究每场具体的革命形势、分析每场革命的经验教训时，都对这些观点进行了详细而具体的阐述。现在，我们将转向他们理论中这无疑是最重要的部分。

A detailed and concrete elaboration of these views was given by Marx and Engels when they studied each particular revolutionary situation, when they analyzed the lessons of the experience of each particular revolution. We shall now pass to this, undoubtedly the most important, part of their theory.

 

 

1848-51年的经验

The Experience of 1848-51

革命前夕

革命总结

马克思在1852年提出的革命问题

The Eve of Revolution

The Revolution Summed Up

The Presentation of the Question by Marx in 1852

1. 革命前夕

1. The Eve of Revolution

马克思主义成熟时期的首批著作—— 《哲学的贫困》和《共产党宣言》——恰好在1848年革命前夕问世。因此，它们除了阐述马克思主义的总体原则外，也在一定程度上反映了当时的具体革命形势。所以，或许更有必要考察这些著作的作者在总结1848-1851年的经验教训之前，对当时的国家状况作了哪些论述。

The first works of mature Marxism — The Poverty of Philosophy and the Communist Manifesto — appeared just on the eve of the revolution of 1848. For this reason, in addition to presenting the general principles of Marxism, they reflect to a certain degree the concrete revolutionary situation of the time. It will, therefore, be more expedient, perhaps, to examine what the authors of these works said about the state immediately before they drew conclusions from the experience of the years 1848-51.

在《哲学的贫困》一书中，马克思写道：

In The Poverty of Philosophy, Marx wrote:

“工人阶级在发展过程中，将以消除阶级及其对抗的联合体取代旧的资产阶级社会，并且不会再有政治权力集团，因为政治权力恰恰是资产阶级社会中阶级对抗的官方表现形式。”

"The working class, in the course of development, will substitute for the old bourgeois society an association which will preclude classes and their antagonism, and there will be no more political power groups, since the political power is precisely the official expression of class antagonism in bourgeois society."

（第182页，德文版，1885年）

(p.182, German edition, 1885)

将这种关于阶级消灭后国家消失的总体阐述与马克思和恩格斯几个月后（确切地说是1847年11月）撰写的《共产党宣言》中所包含的阐述进行比较，会很有启发意义：

It is instructive to compare this general exposition of the idea of the state disappearing after the abolition of classes with the exposition contained in the Communist Manifesto, written by Marx and Engels a few months later - in November 1847, to be exact:

“……在描绘无产阶级发展的各个阶段时，我们追溯了当时社会内部或多或少隐蔽的内战，直到这场内战爆发为公开革命，资产阶级的暴力推翻为无产阶级的统治奠定了基础……

"... In depicting the most general phases of the development of the proletariat, we traced the more or less veiled civil war, raging within existing society up to the point where that war breaks out into open revolution, and where the violent overthrow of the bourgeoisie lays the foundation for the sway of the proletariat....

“……我们上面已经看到，工人阶级革命的第一步是将无产阶级提升到统治阶级的地位，从而赢得民主斗争。

"... We have seen above that the first step in the revolution by the working class is to raise the proletariat to the position of the ruling class to win the battle of democracy.

“无产阶级将利用其政治优势，逐步从资产阶级手中夺取一切资本，将一切生产资料集中到国家手中，即组织起来的无产阶级手中；并尽可能迅速地增加总生产力。”

"The proletariat will use its political supremacy to wrest, by degree, all capital from the bourgeoisie, to centralize all instruments of production in the hands of the state, i.e., of the proletariat organized as the ruling class; and to increase the total productive forces as rapidly as possible."

（第31页和第37页，德文第七版，1906年）

(pp.31 and 37, seventh German edition, 1906)

这里阐述了马克思主义关于国家问题的最杰出、最重要的思想之一，即“无产阶级专政”（马克思和恩格斯在巴黎公社之后开始这样称呼它）的思想；此外，还对国家给出了一个非常有趣的定义，这也是马克思主义中一个“被遗忘的词汇”：“国家，即组织起来的无产阶级作为统治阶级”。

Here we have a formulation of one of the most remarkable and most important ideas of Marxism on the subject of the state, namely, the idea of the "dictatorship of the proletariat" (as Marx and Engels began to call it after the Paris Commune); and, also, a highly interesting definition of the state, which is also one of the "forgotten words" of Marxism: "the state, i.e., the proletariat organized as the ruling class."

在官方社会民主党的宣传鼓动文献中，从未解释过这种国家定义。不仅如此，它还被刻意忽略，因为它与改良主义完全不可调和，是对那些关于“民主和平发展”的常见机会主义偏见和庸俗幻想的当头棒喝。

This definition of the state has never been explained in the prevailing propaganda and agitation literature of the official Social-Democratic parties. More than that, it has been deliberately ignored, for it is absolutely irreconcilable with reformism, and is a slap in the face for the common opportunist prejudices and philistine illusions about the "peaceful development of democracy".

无产阶级需要国家——所有机会主义者、社会沙文主义者和考茨基主义者都反复强调这一点，并向我们保证这是马克思的教导。但他们“忘记”补充一点，首先，根据马克思的理论，无产阶级只需要一个正在消亡的国家，也就是说，一个从一开始就注定要消亡的国家。其次，劳动人民需要一个“国家，即组织起来的无产阶级作为统治阶级”。

The proletariat needs the state — this is repeated by all the opportunists, social-chauvinists and Kautskyites, who assure us that this is what Marx taught. But they "forget" to add that, in the first place, according to Marx, the proletariat needs only a state which is withering away, i.e., a state so constituted that it begins to wither away immediately, and cannot but wither away. And, secondly, the working people need a "state, i.e., the proletariat organized as the ruling class".

国家是一种特殊的武力组织：它是为镇压某个阶级而进行的暴力组织。无产阶级必须镇压哪个阶级？当然，只能是剥削阶级，即资产阶级。劳动人民需要国家，仅仅是为了让国家镇压剥削者的反抗，而只有无产阶级才能领导和执行这种镇压。因为无产阶级是唯一始终坚持革命的阶级，是唯一能够团结所有劳动人民和被剥削人民，共同反对资产阶级，彻底消灭资产阶级的阶级。

The state is a special organization of force: it is an organization of violence for the suppression of some class. What class must the proletariat suppress? Naturally, only the exploiting class, i.e., the bourgeoisie. The working people need the state only to suppress the resistance of the exploiters, and only the proletariat can direct this suppression, can carry it out. For the proletariat is the only class that is consistently revolutionary, the only class that can unite all the working and exploited people in the struggle against the bourgeoisie, in completely removing it.

剥削阶级需要政治统治来维持剥削，即为了少数人的自私利益而损害绝大多数人的利益。被剥削阶级需要政治统治来彻底消除一切剥削，即为了绝大多数人的利益而反对由现代奴隶主——地主和资本家组成的少数人。

The exploiting classes need political rule to maintain exploitation, i.e., in the selfish interests of an insignificant minority against the vast majority of all people. The exploited classes need political rule in order to completely abolish all exploitation, i.e., in the interests of the vast majority of the people, and against the insignificant minority consisting of the modern slave-owners — the landowners and capitalists.

那些小资产阶级民主派，那些用阶级和谐的幻想取代阶级斗争的伪社会主义者，甚至将社会主义转型描绘得如同梦境一般——不是推翻剥削阶级的统治，而是少数人和平地服从于已经意识到自身目标的多数人。这种小资产阶级乌托邦与国家凌驾于阶级之上的观念密不可分，而实践中却导致了工人阶级利益的背叛，例如1848年和1871年的法国大革命的历史，以及世纪之交英国、法国、意大利和其他一些国家的“社会主义者”参与资产阶级内阁的经验都证明了这一点。

The petty-bourgeois democrats, those sham socialists who replaced the class struggle by dreams of class harmony, even pictured the socialist transformation in a dreamy fashion — not as the overthrow of the rule of the exploiting class, but as the peaceful submission of the minority to the majority which has become aware of its aims. This petty-bourgeois utopia, which is inseparable from the idea of the state being above classes, led in practice to the betrayal of the interests of the working classes, as was shown, for example, by the history of the French revolutions of 1848 and 1871, and by the experience of "socialist" participation in bourgeois Cabinets in Britain, France, Italy and other countries at the turn of the century.

马克思一生都在反对小资产阶级社会主义，这种社会主义如今在俄国由社会革命党和孟什维克党复兴。他始终如一地发展自己的阶级斗争理论，直至政治权力理论和国家理论。

All his life Marx fought against this petty-bourgeois socialism, now revived in Russia by the Socialist-Revolutionary and Menshevik parties. He developed his theory of the class struggle consistently, down to the theory of political power, of the state.

推翻资产阶级统治只能由无产阶级完成，无产阶级是特殊的阶级，其生存的经济条件使其具备完成这项任务的能力和力量。资产阶级一边瓦解农民和一切小资产阶级团体，一边却联合、团结、组织无产阶级。只有无产阶级——凭借其在大规模生产中发挥的经济作用——才有能力领导所有劳动人民和被剥削人民。资产阶级剥削、压迫和镇压他们，其程度往往不亚于甚至超过无产阶级，但这些劳动人民和被剥削人民却无力进行独立解放斗争。

The overthrow of bourgeois rule can be accomplished only by the proletariat, the particular class whose economic conditions of existence prepare it for this task and provide it with the possibility and the power to perform it. While the bourgeoisie break up and disintegrate the peasantry and all the petty-bourgeois groups, they weld together, unite and organize the proletariat. Only the proletariat — by virtue of the economic role it plays in large-scale production — is capable of being the leader of all the working and exploited people, whom the bourgeoisie exploit, oppress and crush, often not less but more than they do the proletarians, but who are incapable of waging an independent struggle for their emancipation.

马克思运用阶级斗争理论来论述国家和社会主义革命问题，必然得出关于无产阶级政治统治、无产阶级专政（即人民武装力量直接支持的统一政权）的结论。只有无产阶级成为统治阶级，能够镇压资产阶级不可避免的、绝望的抵抗，并组织全体劳动人民和被剥削人民投身于新的经济制度，才能推翻资产阶级。

The theory of class struggle, applied by Marx to the question of the state and the socialist revolution, leads as a matter of course to the recognition of the political rule of the proletariat, of its dictatorship, i.e., of undivided power directly backed by the armed force of the people. The overthrow of the bourgeoisie can be achieved only by the proletariat becoming the ruling class, capable of crushing the inevitable and desperate resistance of the bourgeoisie, and of organizing all the working and exploited people for the new economic system.

无产阶级需要国家政权、集中力量的组织、暴力的组织，既要镇压剥削者的抵抗，又要领导广大人民群众——农民、小资产阶级和半无产阶级——从事社会主义经济的组织工作。

The proletariat needs state power, a centralized organization of force, an organization of violence, both to crush the resistance of the exploiters and to lead the enormous mass of the population — the peasants, the petty bourgeoisie, and semi-proletarians — in the work of organizing a socialist economy.

通过教育工人党，马克思主义培养无产阶级先锋队，使他们能够掌握政权，领导全体人民走向社会主义，指导和组织新制度，成为全体劳动人民和被剥削人民组织社会生活、摆脱资产阶级、反对资产阶级的教师、向导和领导者。相反，现今盛行的机会主义却把工人党成员训练成高收入工人的代表，这些人脱离群众，在资本主义制度下“过得相当不错”，为了蝇头小利而出卖自己的天职，即放弃自己作为人民革命领袖反对资产阶级的角色。

By educating the workers' party, Marxism educates the vanguard of the proletariat, capable of assuming power and leading the whole people to socialism, of directing and organizing the new system, of being the teacher, the guide, the leader of all the working and exploited people in organizing their social life without the bourgeoisie and against the bourgeoisie. By contrast, the opportunism now prevailing trains the members of the workers' party to be the representatives of the better-paid workers, who lose touch with the masses, "get along" fairly well under capitalism, and sell their birthright for a mass of pottage, i.e., renounce their role as revolutionary leaders of the people against the bourgeoisie.

马克思关于“国家，即组织起来的无产阶级作为统治阶级”的理论，与他关于无产阶级在历史上的革命作用的整个理论密不可分。这一统治的最终目标是无产阶级专政，即无产阶级的政治统治。

Marx's theory of "the state, i.e., the proletariat organized as the ruling class", is inseparably bound up with the whole of his doctrine of the revolutionary role of the proletariat in history. The culmination of this rule is the proletarian dictatorship, the political rule of the proletariat.

但是，既然无产阶级需要国家作为一种特殊的暴力组织形式来反对资产阶级，那么自然而然就会得出这样的结论：如果不先废除、摧毁资产阶级为自己建立的国家机器，这样的组织又怎能建立起来呢？《共产党宣言》直接指向这个结论，马克思在总结1848-1851年革命的经验时，也正是谈到了这个结论。

But since the proletariat needs the state as a special form of organization of violence against the bourgeoisie, the following conclusion suggests itself: is it conceivable that such an organization can be created without first abolishing, destroying the state machine created by the bourgeoisie for themselves? The Communist Manifesto leads straight to this conclusion, and it is of this conclusion that Marx speaks when summing up the experience of the revolution of 1848-51.



 



 

2. 革命概述

2. The Revolution Summed Up

马克思在《路易·波拿巴的雾月十八日》中，就我们所讨论的国家问题，总结了他从1848-1851年革命中得出的结论，如下论述：

Marx sums up his conclusions from the revolution of 1848-51, on the subject of the state we are concerned with, in the following argument contained in The Eighteenth Brumaire of Louis Bonaparte:

“但革命是彻底的。它仍在炼狱中跋涉。它有条不紊地进行着。到1851年12月2日（路易·波拿巴发动政变之日），它已经完成了一半的准备工作。现在，它正在完成另一半。首先，它完善了议会权力，以便能够推翻它。现在，它已经实现了这一点，它正在完善行政权力，将其简化到最纯粹的形式，孤立它，让它成为唯一的目标，以便集中所有破坏力量来对付它。当它完成这后半部分的准备工作时，欧洲将会从座位上跳起来，欢呼雀跃：干得好，老鼹鼠！”

"But the revolution is throughgoing. It is still journeying through purgatory. It does its work methodically. By December 2, 1851 [the day of Louis Bonaparte's coup d'etat], it had completed one half of its preparatory work. It is now completing the other half. First it perfected the parliamentary power, in order to be able to overthrow it. Now that it has attained this, it is perfecting the executive power, reducing it to its purest expression, isolating it, setting it up against itself as the sole object, in order to concentrate all its forces of destruction against it. And when it has done this second half of its preliminary work, Europe will leap from its seat and exultantly exclaim: well grubbed, old mole!

“这个拥有庞大官僚和军事组织的行政权力机构，拥有庞大而精巧的国家机器，拥有五十万官员，以及五十万军队，这个可怕的寄生虫般的机构，它渗透到法国社会的各个角落，堵塞其所有毛孔，它兴起于君主专制时期，伴随着封建制度的衰落，并加速了这一衰落。”第一次法国大革命发展了中央集权，“但与此同时”，它也扩大了“政府权力的代理人的范围、属性和数量。拿破仑完善了这一国家机器”。合法君主制和七月王朝“除了进一步细分劳动之外，没有增加任何其他内容”。

"This executive power with its enormous bureaucratic and military organization, with its vast and ingenious state machinery, with a host of officials numbering half a million, besides an army of another half million, this appalling parasitic body, which enmeshes the body of French society and chokes all its pores, sprang up in the days of the absolute monarchy, with the decay of the feudal system, which it helped to hasten." The first French Revolution developed centralization, "but at the same time" it increased "the extent, the attributes and the number of agents of governmental power. Napoleon completed this state machinery". The legitimate monarchy and the July monarchy "added nothing but a greater division of labor"....

“……最终，在与革命的斗争中，议会共和国发现自己不得不采取镇压措施的同时，加强政府的资源和权力集中化。所有革命都使这台机器更加完善，而不是摧毁它。争夺统治权的各党派都将对这座庞大国家机器的控制视为胜利者的主要战利品。”

"... Finally, in its struggle against the revolution, the parliamentary republic found itself compelled to strengthen, along with repressive measures, the resources and centralization of governmental power. All revolutions perfected this machine instead of smashing it. The parties that contended in turn for domination regarded the possession of this huge state edifice as the principal spoils of the victor."

（《路易·波拿巴的雾月十八日》 ，

第98-99页，第四版，汉堡，1907年）

(The Eighteenth Brumaire of Louis Bonaparte

pp.98-99, fourth edition, Hamburg, 1907)

在这一非凡的论证中，马克思主义相比《共产党宣言》向前迈出了巨大的一步。《共产党宣言》中，国家问题仍然以极其抽象的方式，用最笼统的术语和表达来处理。而在上述引文中，这个问题得到了具体的阐述，结论也极其精确、明确、实用且切实可感：以往所有的革命都完善了国家机器，而它必须被摧毁、粉碎。

In this remarkable argument, Marxism takes a tremendous step forward compared with the Communist Manifesto. In the latter, the question of the state is still treated in an extremely abstract manner, in the most general terms and expressions. In the above-quoted passage, the question is treated in a concrete manner, and the conclusion is extremely precise, definite, practical and palpable: all previous revolutions perfected the state machine, whereas it must be broken, smashed.

这一结论是马克思主义国家理论的主要和根本要点。而正是这一根本要点被占主导地位的官方社会民主党完全忽视，甚至被第二国际最重要的理论家卡尔·考茨基歪曲（我们稍后会看到）。

This conclusion is the chief and fundamental point in the Marxist theory of the state. And it is precisely this fundamental point which has been completely ignored by the dominant official Social-Democratic parties and, indeed, distorted (as we shall see later) by the foremost theoretician of the Second International, Karl Kautsky.

《共产党宣言》对历史进行了概括，迫使我们把国家视为阶级统治的工具，并最终得出必然的结论：无产阶级若不先夺取政权、取得政治统治地位、将国家改造为“以无产阶级为统治阶级的组织”，就无法推翻资产阶级；而这个无产阶级国家在取得胜利后会立即开始消亡，因为在一个没有阶级斗争的社会里，国家是不必要的，也是不可能存在的。至于从历史发展的角度来看，资产阶级国家如何被无产阶级国家所取代，这里并没有讨论。

The Communist Manifesto gives a general summary of history, which compels us to regard the state as the organ of class rule and leads us to the inevitable conclusion that the proletariat cannot overthrow the bourgeoisie without first winning political power, without attaining political supremacy, without transforming the state into the "proletariat organized as the ruling class"; and that this proletarian state will begin to wither away immediately after its victory because the state is unnecessary and cannot exist in a society in which there are no class antagonisms. The question as to how, from the point of view of historical development, the replacement of the bourgeois by the proletarian state is to take place is not raised here.

这是马克思在1852年提出并解答的问题。马克思秉持辩证唯物主义哲学，以1848年至1851年革命伟大岁月的历史经验为基础。在这里，如同在其他任何地方一样，他的理论是对经验的总结，并受到深刻的哲学世界观和丰富的历史知识的启发。

This is the question Marx raises and answers in 1852. True to his philosophy of dialectical materialism, Marx takes as his basis the historical experience of the great years of revolution, 1848 to 1851. Here, as everywhere else, his theory is a summing up of experience, illuminated by a profound philosophical conception of the world and a rich knowledge of history.

具体而言，国家问题在于：资产阶级国家，即资产阶级统治所必需的国家机器，是如何在历史上产生的？在资产阶级革命过程中以及面对被压迫阶级的独立行动时，它经历了哪些变化，发生了哪些演变？无产阶级与这个国家机器的关系是什么？

The problem of the state is put specifically: How did the bourgeois state, the state machine necessary for the rule of the bourgeoisie, come into being historically? What changes did it undergo, what evolution did it perform in the course of bourgeois revolutions and in the face of the independent actions of the oppressed classes? What are the tasks of the proletariat in relation to this state machine?

资产阶级社会特有的中央集权国家权力是在专制主义垮台时期产生的。这一国家机器最显著的两个特征是官僚机构和常备军。马克思和恩格斯在他们的著作中反复指出，资产阶级与这些机构之间有着千丝万缕的联系。每一个工人的经验都以极其生动形象的方式展现了这种联系。工人阶级正是从自身的惨痛经历中认识到这种联系的。正因如此，他们才如此轻易地理解并牢牢地接受了这一联系必然性的理论，而小资产阶级民主派要么愚昧轻率地否认这一理论，要么更加轻率地“泛泛地”承认，却忘记得出相应的实践结论。

The centralized state power that is peculiar to bourgeois society came into being in the period of the fall of absolutism. Two institutions most characteristic of this state machine are the bureaucracy and the standing army. In their works, Marx and Engels repeatedly show that the bourgeoisie are connected with these institutions by thousands of threads. Every worker's experience illustrates this connection in an extremely graphic and impressive manner. From its own bitter experience, the working class learns to recognize this connection. That is why it so easily grasps and so firmly learns the doctrine which shows the inevitability of this connection, a doctrine which the petty-bourgeois democrats either ignorantly and flippantly deny, or still more flippantly admit "in general", while forgetting to draw appropriate practical conclusions.

官僚机构和常备军是资产阶级社会肌体上的“寄生虫”——这种寄生虫是由撕裂社会的内部矛盾所滋生的，但它却“扼杀”了社会的所有生命之源。如今在官方社会民主党中盛行的考茨基式机会主义认为，国家是寄生生物的观点是无政府主义特有的、专属的属性。毋庸置疑，这种对马克思主义的歪曲对那些庸俗之徒大有裨益，他们将社会主义贬低到前所未有的地步，用“保卫祖国”的概念来为帝国主义战争辩护和美化；但这无疑仍然是一种歪曲。

The bureaucracy and the standing army are a "parasite" on the body of bourgeois society - a parasite created by the internal antagonisms which rend that society, but a parasite which "chokes" all its vital pores. The Kautskyite opportunism now prevailing in official Social-Democracy considers the view that the state is a parasitic organism to be the peculiar and exclusive attribute of anarchism. It goes without saying that this distortion of Marxism is of vast advantage to those philistines who have reduced socialism to the unheard-of disgrace of justifying and prettifying the imperialist war by applying to it the concept of "defence of the fatherland"; but it is unquestionably a distortion, nevertheless.

自封建制度崩溃以来，欧洲经历了无数次资产阶级革命，而官僚和军事机构的发展、完善和强化贯穿始终。尤其值得注意的是，正是这套机构吸引着小资产阶级，使他们倒向大资产阶级，并在很大程度上受其控制。这套机构为农民、小工匠、商人等上层阶级提供了相对舒适、安逸和体面的工作，使这些职位持有者凌驾于人民之上。想想1917年2月27日之后的六个月里俄国发生了什么。以前优先分配给黑衣党的官职，现在都落入了立宪民主党、孟什维克和社会革命党的手中。没有人真正考虑过进行任何严肃的改革。他们竭尽全力地将改革推迟到“立宪会议召开之后”，并不断地将立宪会议的召开推迟到战后！但是，在瓜分部长、副部长、总督等这些高薪职位这件事上，却丝毫没有拖延，也没有等待制宪会议！组建政府过程中上演的种种权谋游戏，本质上不过是这种瓜分和重新分配“战利品”的体现，这种瓜分和重新分配早已在全国各地、中央和地方政府的各个部门进行。1917年2月27日至8月27日这六个月，可以概括为：改革被搁置，官职分配完成，而分配中的“错误”则通过几次重新分配得以纠正。

The development, perfection, and strengthening of the bureaucratic and military apparatus proceeded during all the numerous bourgeois revolutions which Europe has witnessed since the fall of feudalism. In particular, it is the petty bourgeois who are attracted to the side of the big bourgeoisie and are largely subordinated to them through this apparatus, which provides the upper sections of the peasants, small artisans, tradesmen, and the like with comparatively comfortable, quiet, and respectable jobs raising the holders above the people. Consider what happened in Russia during the six months following February 27, 1917. The official posts which formerly were given by preference to the Black Hundreds have now become the spoils of the Cadets, Mensheviks, and Social-Revolutionaries. Nobody has really thought of introducing any serious reforms. Every effort has been made to put them off "until the Constituent Assembly meets", and to steadily put off its convocation until after the war! But there has been no delay, no waiting for the Constituent Assembly, in the matter of dividing the spoils of getting the lucrative jobs of ministers, deputy ministers, governors-general, etc., etc.! The game of combinations that has been played in forming the government has been, in essence, only an expression of this division and redivision of the "spoils", which has been going on above and below, throughout the country, in every department of central and local government. The six months between February 27 and August 27, 1917, can be summed up, objectively summed up beyond all dispute, as follows: reforms shelved, distribution of official jobs accomplished and "mistakes" in the distribution corrected by a few redistributions.

但是，官僚机构越是在各个资产阶级和小资产阶级政党（例如俄国的立宪民主党、社会革命党和孟什维克党）之间“重新分配”，被压迫阶级及其领导的无产阶级就越发清楚地意识到，他们与整个资产阶级社会之间存在着不可调和的敌意。因此，所有资产阶级政党，即使是最民主的、最“革命民主”的政党，也必须加强对革命无产阶级的镇压措施，强化强制机器，即国家机器。这一事态发展迫使革命“集中一切破坏力量”来对抗国家政权，其目标不再是完善国家机器，而是摧毁它。

But the more the bureaucratic apparatus is "redistributed" among the various bourgeois and petty-bourgeois parties (among the Cadets, Socialist-Revolutionaries and Mensheviks in the case of Russia), the more keenly aware the oppressed classes, and the proletariat at their head, become of their irreconcilable hostility to the whole of bourgeois society. Hence the need for all bourgeois parties, even for the most democratic and "revolutionary-democratic" among them, to intensify repressive measures against the revolutionary proletariat, to strengthen the apparatus of coercion, i.e., the state machine. This course of events compels the revolution "to concentrate all its forces of destruction" against the state power, and to set itself the aim, not of improving the state machine, but of smashing and destroying it.

促使人们以这种方式阐述这一问题的，并非逻辑推理，而是实际的发展，是1848年至1851年间的实际经验。马克思对坚实的历史经验基础的坚持程度，可以从以下事实看出：1852年，他尚未明确提出什么将取代被摧毁的国家机器。经验尚未提供处理这一问题的素材，而历史后来在1871年将这个问题提上了议程。1852年，能够通过科学观察精确地确定的，仅仅是无产阶级革命已经接近于“集中一切破坏力量”对抗国家政权，即“摧毁”国家机器的任务。

It was not logical reasoning, but actual developments, the actual experience of 1848-51, that led to the matter being presented in this way. The extent to which Marx held strictly to the solid ground of historical experience can be seen from the fact that, in 1852, he did not yet specifically raise the question of what was to take the place of the state machine to be destroyed. Experience had not yet provided material for dealing with this question, which history placed on the agenda later on, in 1871. In 1852, all that could be established with the accuracy of scientific observation was that the proletarian revolution had approached the task of "concentrating all its forces of destruction" against the state power, of "smashing" the state machine.

这里可能会出现一个问题：将马克思的经验、观察和结论推广到比1848-1851年这三年法国历史更广阔的领域是否正确？在探讨这个问题之前，让我们先回顾一下恩格斯说过的一句话，然后再考察一下事实。

Here the question may arise: is it correct to generalize the experience, observations and conclusions of Marx, to apply them to a field that is wider than the history of France during the three years 1848-51? Before proceeding to deal with this question, let us recall a remark made by Engels and then examine the facts.

恩格斯在《雾月十八日》第三版的序言中写道：

In his introduction to the third edition of The Eighteenth Brumaire, Engels wrote:

“法国是历史上阶级斗争最为彻底的国家，每一次都打到了最后，因此，阶级斗争发生并最终体现的政治形态也在这里留下了最为鲜明的印记。作为中世纪封建主义的中心，自文艺复兴以来，法国一直是建立在社会等级基础上的统一君主制的典范。然而，法国在大革命中摧毁了封建制度，并建立了资产阶级统治，其纯粹程度之高，在欧洲其他任何国家都无与伦比。而在这里，向上奋斗的无产阶级反对统治资产阶级的斗争，也以其他任何地方都未曾出现过的尖锐形式展现出来。”

"France is the country where, more than anywhere else, the historical class struggles were each time fought out to a finish, and where, consequently, the changing political forms within which they move and in which their results are summarized have been stamped in the sharpest outlines. The centre of feudalism in the Middle Ages, the model country, since the Renaissance, of a unified monarchy based on social estates, France demolished feudalism in the Great Revolution and established the rule of the bourgeoisie in a classical purity unequalled by any other European land. And the struggle of the upward-striving proletariat against the ruling bourgeoisie appeared here in an acute form unknown elsewhere."

（1907年版，第4页）

(p.4, 1907 edition)

最后那句话已经过时了，因为自 1871 年以来，法国无产阶级的革命斗争一直处于平静期，尽管这种平静期可能很长，但这丝毫不能排除在即将到来的无产阶级革命中，法国可能会成为阶级斗争彻底结束的经典国家的可能性。

The last remark is out of date insomuch as since 1871 there has been a lull in the revolutionary struggle of the French proletariat, although, long as this lull may be, it does not at all preclude the possibility that in the coming proletarian revolution France may show herself to be the classic country of the class struggle to a finish.

然而，让我们纵览一下世纪之交发达国家的历史。我们会发现，同样的进程以更为缓慢、更为多样的形式在更为广阔的范围内展开：一方面，共和制国家（法国、美国、瑞士）和君主制国家（英国、一定程度上的德国、意大利、斯堪的纳维亚国家等）都出现了“议会权力”的发展；另一方面，各种资产阶级和小资产阶级政党之间展开了权力斗争，不断分配和重新分配官职的“战利品”，而资产阶级社会的基础却未发生改变；最后，行政权力及其官僚和军事机构也得到了完善和巩固。

Let us, however, cast a general glance over the history of the advanced countries at the turn of the century. We shall see that the same process went on more slowly, in more varied forms, in a much wider field: on the one hand, the development of "parliamentary power" both in the republican countries (France, America, Switzerland), and in the monarchies (Britain, Germany to a certain extent, Italy, the Scandinavia countries, etc.); on the other hand, a struggle for power among the various bourgeois and petty-bourgeois parties which distributed and redistributed the "spoils" of office, with the foundations of bourgeois society unchanged; and, lastly, the perfection and consolidation of the "executive power", of its bureaucratic and military apparatus.

毫无疑问，这些特征是所有资本主义国家现代发展进程的共同特征。在1848年至1851年的最后三年里，法国以迅速、显著和集中的方式展现了整个资本主义世界特有的发展进程。

There is not the slightest doubt that these features are common to the whole of the modern evolution of all capitalist states in general. In the last three years 1848-51 France displayed, in a swift, sharp, concentrated form, the very same processes of development which are peculiar to the whole capitalist world.

帝国主义——银行资本时代、巨型资本主义垄断时代、垄断资本主义发展为国家垄断资本主义的时代——在君主制国家和最自由的共和制国家，都伴随着对无产阶级镇压措施的加强，其官僚和军事机构也出现了前所未有的增长。

Imperialism - the era of bank capital, the era of gigantic capitalist monopolies, of the development of monopoly capitalism into state- monopoly capitalism - has clearly shown an unprecedented growth in its bureaucratic and military apparatus in connection with the intensification of repressive measures against the proletariat both in the monarchical and in the freest, republican countries.

世界历史现在无疑正以比 1852 年更大的规模，将无产阶级革命的所有力量集中起来，以摧毁国家机器为目标。

World history is now undoubtedly leading, on an incomparably larger scale than in 1852, to the "concentration of all the forces" of the proletarian revolution on the "destruction" of the state machine.

无产阶级将用什么来取代它，巴黎公社提供的极具启发性的资料就说明了这一点。

What the proletariat will put in its place is suggested by the highly instructive material furnished by the Paris Commune.



 



 

3. 马克思在1852年提出的这个问题

3. The Presentation of the Question by Marx in 1852

1907年，梅林在《新时代》（第25卷，第2期，第164页）上发表了马克思1852年3月5日写给魏德迈耶的信的节选。这封信中包含以下值得注意的观点：

In 1907, Mehring, in the magazine Neue Zeit (Vol.XXV, 2, p.164), published extracts from Marx's letter to Weydemeyer dated March 5, 1852. This letter, among other things, contains the following remarkable observation:

“至于我自己，发现现代社会阶级的存在以及阶级斗争并非我的功劳。早在我之前，资产阶级历史学家就已描述了阶级斗争的历史发展，资产阶级经济学家也已阐述了阶级的经济结构。我的创新之处在于证明了：（1）阶级的存在仅仅与生产发展的特定历史阶段相关；（2）阶级斗争必然导致无产阶级专政；（3）无产阶级专政本身只是向废除一切阶级、建立无阶级社会过渡的阶段。”

"And now as to myself, no credit is due to me for discovering the existence of classes in modern society or the struggle between them. Long before me bourgeois historians had described the historical development of this class struggle and bourgeois economists, the economic anatomy of classes. What I did that was new was to prove: (1) that the existence of classes is only bound up with the particular, historical phases in the development of production (historische Entwicklungsphasen der Produktion), (2) that the class struggle necessarily leads to the dictatorship of the proletariat, (3) that this dictatorship itself only constitutes the transition to the abolition of all classes and to a classless society."

马克思用这些话，首先清晰地表达了他的理论与资产阶级最杰出、最深刻的思想家的理论之间的主要和根本区别；其次，表达了他的国家理论的本质。

In these words, Marx succeeded in expressing with striking clarity, first, the chief and radical difference between his theory and that of the foremost and most profound thinkers of the bourgeoisie; and, secondly, the essence of his theory of the state.

人们常说，马克思理论的核心是阶级斗争。但这是错误的。这种错误的观念往往导致对马克思主义的机会主义歪曲，并以资产阶级可接受的方式对其进行歪曲。因为阶级斗争理论并非马克思所创，而是马克思之前的资产阶级所创，而且，总的来说，它是资产阶级所接受的。那些只承认阶级斗争的人还不是马克思主义者；他们仍然囿于资产阶级思想和资产阶级政治的框架之内。将马克思主义局限于阶级斗争理论，就等于限制马克思主义，歪曲它，将其简化为资产阶级可以接受的东西。只有将对阶级斗争的认识扩展到对无产阶级专政的认识，才是真正的马克思主义者。这才是马克思主义者与普通小资产阶级（以及大资产阶级）之间最深刻的区别。这是检验对马克思主义的真正理解和认识的试金石。毫不奇怪，当欧洲历史将工人阶级作为一个实际问题逼到这一境地时，不仅所有机会主义者和改良主义者，而且所有考茨基主义者（那些在改良主义和马克思主义之间摇摆不定的人）都暴露出其卑鄙无知和背弃无产阶级专政的小资产阶级民主主义本质。考茨基的小册子《无产阶级专政》出版于1918年8月，也就是本书第一版出版很久之后，正是小资产阶级歪曲马克思主义、在行动上卑鄙地背弃马克思主义，却在口头上虚伪地承认马克思主义的完美例证（参见我的小册子《无产阶级革命与叛徒考茨基》，彼得格勒和莫斯科，1918年）。

It is often said and written that the main point in Marx's theory is the class struggle. But this is wrong. And this wrong notion very often results in an opportunist distortion of Marxism and its falsification in a spirit acceptable to the bourgeoisie. For the theory of the class struggle was created not by Marx, but by the bourgeoisie before Marx, and, generally speaking, it is acceptable to the bourgeoisie. Those who recognize only the class struggle are not yet Marxists; they may be found to be still within the bounds of bourgeois thinking and bourgeois politics. To confine Marxism to the theory of the class struggle means curtailing Marxism, distorting it, reducing it to something acceptable to the bourgeoisie. Only he is a Marxist who extends the recognition of the class struggle to the recognition of the dictatorship of the proletariat. That is what constitutes the most profound distinction between the Marxist and the ordinary petty (as well as big) bourgeois. This is the touchstone on which the real understanding and recognition of Marxism should be tested. And it is not surprising that when the history of Europe brought the working class face to face with this question as a practical issue, not only all the opportunists and reformists, but all the Kautskyites (people who vacillate between reformism and Marxism) proved to be miserable philistines and petty-bourgeois democrats repudiating the dictatorship of the proletariat. Kautsky's pamphlet, The Dictatorship of the Proletariat, published in August 1918, i.e., long after the first edition of the present book, is a perfect example of petty-bourgeois distortion of Marxism and base renunciation of it in deeds, while hypocritically recognizing it in words (see my pamphlet, The Proletarian Revolution and the Renegade Kautsky, Petrograd and Moscow, 1918).

当今的机会主义，以它的主要代言人、前马克思主义者卡尔·考茨基为代表，与马克思上述对资产阶级立场的描述完全吻合，因为这种机会主义将阶级斗争的认识局限于资产阶级关系的范畴。（在这个范畴内，在这个框架内，没有一个受过教育的自由主义者会“原则上”否认阶级斗争的存在！）机会主义没有将阶级斗争的认识扩展到最根本的层面，即从资本主义向共产主义过渡的时期，即推翻和彻底消灭资产阶级的时期。事实上，这一时期必然是一个阶级斗争空前激烈、形式空前尖锐的时期，因此，在这一时期，国家必然会以一种新的方式成为民主国家（为了无产阶级和所有无产者），并以一种新的方式成为专制国家（为了资产阶级）。
