Opportunism today, as represented by its principal spokesman, the ex-Marxist Karl Kautsky, fits in completely with Marx's characterization of the bourgeois position quoted above, for this opportunism limits recognition of the class struggle to the sphere of bourgeois relations. (Within this sphere, within its framework, not a single educated liberal will refuse to recognize the class struggle "in principle"!) Opportunism does not extend recognition of the class struggle to the cardinal point, to the period of transition from capitalism to communism, of the overthrow and the complete abolition of the bourgeoisie. In reality, this period inevitably is a period of an unprecedently violent class struggle in unprecedentedly acute forms, and, consequently, during this period the state must inevitably be a state that is democratic in a new way (for the proletariat and the propertyless in general) and dictatorial in a new way (against the bourgeoisie).

此外，只有那些认识到单一阶级专政不仅对任何阶级社会都是必要的，不仅对推翻资产阶级的无产阶级而言也是必要的，而且对从资本主义到“无阶级社会”再到共产主义的整个历史时期而言也是必要的，才能真正掌握马克思国家理论的精髓。资产阶级国家的形式千差万别，但其本质却是一样的：所有这些国家，无论其形式如何，归根结底都必然是资产阶级专政。从资本主义向共产主义的过渡必然会产生极其丰富多样的政治形式，但其本质必然是相同的：那就是无产阶级专政。

Further. The essence of Marx's theory of the state has been mastered only by those who realize that the dictatorship of a single class is necessary not only for every class society in general, not only for the proletariat which has overthrown the bourgeoisie, but also for the entire historical period which separates capitalism from "classless society", from communism. Bourgeois states are most varied in form, but their essence is the same: all these states, whatever their form, in the final analysis are inevitably the dictatorship of the bourgeoisie. The transition from capitalism to communism is certainly bound to yield a tremendous abundance and variety of political forms, but the essence will inevitably be the same: the dictatorship of the proletariat.

1871年巴黎公社的经验：马克思的分析

Experience of the Paris Commune of 1871. Marx's Analysis

是什么让公社社员的尝试显得英勇？

什么将取代被摧毁的国家机器？

废除议会制；

建立民族团结组织；

废除寄生国家

What Made the Communards' Attempt Heroic?

What is to Replace the Smashed State Machine?

Abolition of Parliamentarism

Organisation of National Unity

Aboloition of the Parasite State

 

 

1. 是什么让公社社员的尝试成为英雄之举？

1. What Made the Communards' Attempt Heroic?

众所周知，1870年秋，也就是巴黎公社成立前几个月，马克思曾警告巴黎工人，任何推翻政府的企图都是绝望的愚蠢之举。然而，1871年3月，当一场决定性的战斗被迫降临到工人身上，而他们也接受了这一现实，当起义成为既成事实时，尽管有不祥的预兆，马克思仍然以极大的热情迎接无产阶级革命。马克思并没有像臭名昭著的俄国马克思主义叛徒普列汉诺夫那样，坚持以迂腐的态度谴责这场“不合时宜”的运动。普列汉诺夫在1905年11月曾撰文鼓励工人和农民的斗争，但在1905年12月之后，他却以自由主义者的口吻高呼：“他们不应该拿起武器。”

It is well known that in the autumn of 1870, a few months before the Commune, Marx warned the Paris workers that any attempt to overthrow the government would be the folly of despair. But when, in March 1871, a decisive battle was forced upon the workers and they accepted it, when the uprising had become a fact, Marx greeted the proletarian revolution with the greatest enthusiasm, in spite of unfavorable auguries. Marx did not persist in the pedantic attitude of condemning an "untimely" movement as did the ill-famed Russian renegade from marxism, Plekhanov, who in November 1905 wrote encouragingly about the workers' and peasants' struggle, but after December 1905 cried, liberal fashion: "They should not have taken up arms."

然而，马克思不仅对公社社员的英勇事迹充满热情——正如他所说，他们“攻破了天庭”。尽管群众革命运动未能实现其目标，但他仍然将其视为一次极其重要的历史经验，是世界无产阶级革命的一次重大进步，是比数百个纲领和论证更为重要的实践步骤。马克思努力分析这一实验，从中汲取策略经验，并以此为依据重新审视自己的理论。

Marx, however, was not only enthusiastic about the heroism of the Communards, who, as he expressed it, "stormed heaven". Although the mass revolutionary movement did not achieve its aim, he regarded it as a historic experience of enormous importance, as a certain advance of the world proletarian revolution, as a practical step that was more important than hundreds of programmes and arguments. Marx endeavored to analyze this experiment, to draw tactical lessons from it and re-examine his theory in the light of it.

马克思认为有必要对《共产党宣言》进行的唯一“修正”，是根据巴黎公社的革命经验而作出的。

The only "correction" Marx thought it necessary to make to the Communist Manifesto he made on the basis of the revolutionary experience of the Paris Commune.

《共产党宣言》新德文版的最后一篇序言，由两位作者共同签署，日期为1872年6月24日。在这篇序言中，作者卡尔·马克思和弗里德里希·恩格斯指出，《共产党宣言》的纲领“在某些细节上已经过时”，并继续说道：

The last preface to the new German edition of the Communist Manifesto, signed by both its authors, is dated June 24, 1872. In this preface the authors, Karl Marx and Frederick Engels, say that the programme of the Communist Manifesto "has in some details become out-of-date", and the go on to say:

“……公社尤其证明了一件事，那就是‘工人阶级不能简单地夺取现成的国家机器并为己所用’……”

"... One thing especially was proved by the Commune, viz., that 'the working class cannot simply lay hold of the ready-made state machinery and wield it for its own purposes'...."

作者从马克思的著作《法兰西内战》中摘取了这段文字中用单引号括起来的部分。

The authors took the words that are in single quotation marks in this passage from Marx's book, The Civil War in France.

因此，马克思和恩格斯认为巴黎公社的一个主要和根本教训具有极其重要的意义，以至于他们将其作为一项重要的修正引入了《共产党宣言》。

Thus, Marx and Engels regarded one principal and fundamental lesson of the Paris Commune as being of such enormous importance that they introduced it as an important correction into the Communist Manifesto.

最典型的是，正是这一重要的修正被机会主义者歪曲了，其含义可能连《共产党宣言》的读者中至少有十分之九，甚至百分之九千九百的读者都不了解。我们将在后面专门讨论歪曲的章节中更详细地探讨这种歪曲。这里只需指出，目前对马克思刚才引述的那段著名论述的庸俗“解读”是，马克思在这里强调的是缓慢发展，以此来反驳夺取政权的理念，等等。

Most characteristically, it is this important correction that has been distorted by the opportunists, and its meaning probably is not known to nine-tenths, if not ninety-nine-hundredths, of the readers of the Communist Manifesto. We shall deal with this distortion more fully farther on, in a chapter devoted specially to distortions. Here it will be sufficient to note that the current, vulgar "interpretation" of Marx's famous statement just quoted is that Marx here allegedly emphasizes the idea of slow development in contradistinction to the seizure of power, and so on.

事实上，情况恰恰相反。马克思的观点是，工人阶级必须瓦解、摧毁“现成的国家机器”，而不仅仅满足于夺取它。

As a matter of fact, the exact opposite is the case. Marx's idea is that the working class must break up, smash the "ready-made state machinery", and not confine itself merely to laying hold of it.

1871年4月12日，也就是巴黎公社成立之时，马克思写信给库格尔曼：

On April 12, 1871, i.e., just at the time of the Commune, Marx wrote to Kugelmann:

“如果你翻阅我的《雾月十八日》最后一章，你会发现我宣称，法国大革命的下一次尝试将不再像以前那样，是将官僚军事机器从一人手中转移到另一人手中，而是要将其摧毁（马克思的斜体字——原文是zerbrechen），这是欧洲大陆所有真正人民革命的前提。而这正是我们在巴黎英勇的党内同志们正在努力的方向。”

"If you look up the last chapter of my Eighteenth Brumaire, you will find that I declare that the next attempt of the French Revolution will be no longer, as before, to transfer the bureaucratic-military machine from one hand to another, but to smash it [Marx's italics - the original is zerbrechen], and this is the precondition for every real people's revolution on the Continent. And this is what our heroic Party comrades in Paris are attempting."

（《新时代周报》，第20卷，第1期，1901-02年，第709页。）

（马克思写给库格尔曼的信件至少有两个俄文版本，其中一个版本由我编辑并作序。）

(Neue Zeit, Vol.XX, 1, 1901-02, p.709.)

(The letters of Marx to Kugelmann have appeared in Russian in no less than two editions, one of which I edited and supplied with a preface.)

“摧毁官僚军事机器”这句话，简明扼要地概括了马克思主义关于无产阶级在革命中与国家关系的主要任务。而这一教训不仅被完全忽视，而且还被盛行的考茨基主义马克思主义“解释”彻底歪曲了！

The words, "to smash the bureaucratic-military machine", briefly express the principal lesson of Marxism regarding the tasks of the proletariat during a revolution in relation to the state. And this is the lesson that has been not only completely ignored, but positively distorted by the prevailing, Kautskyite, "interpretation" of Marxism!

至于马克思对《雾月十八日》的引用，我们已在上面完整引用了相关段落。

As for Marx's reference to The Eighteenth Brumaire, we have quoted the relevant passage in full above.

值得注意的是，马克思上述论证中有两点值得关注。首先，他将结论限定于欧洲大陆。这在1871年是可以理解的，当时的英国仍是纯粹资本主义国家的典范，但它没有军国主义集团，而且在很大程度上也没有官僚机构。因此，马克思将英国排除在外，因为当时的英国似乎有可能爆发革命，甚至爆发人民革命，而无需以摧毁“现成的国家机器”为前提。

It is interesting to note, in particular, two points in the above-quoted argument of Marx. First, he restricts his conclusion to the Continent. This was understandable in 1871, when Britain was still the model of a purely capitalist country, but without a militarist clique and, to a considerable degree, without a bureaucracy. Marx therefore excluded Britain, where a revolution, even a people's revolution, then seemed possible, and indeed was possible, without the precondition of destroying "ready-made state machinery".

今天，在1917年，第一次帝国主义大战爆发之际，马克思的这一限制已不再有效。英国和美国，这两个曾经是盎格鲁-撒克逊“自由”（指没有军国主义集团和官僚机构）的最大也是最后的代表——在全世界范围内——如今已彻底陷入了欧洲普遍存在的肮脏血腥的官僚军事机构泥潭，这些机构凌驾于一切之上，压制一切。今天，在英国和美国，“任何真正的人民革命的前提条件”也是摧毁“现成的国家机器”（这些机器在1914年至1917年间于这些国家被制造出来，并发展到符合“欧洲”普遍帝国主义的完美状态）。

Today, in 1917, at the time of the first great imperialist war, this restriction made by Marx is no longer valid. Both Britain and America, the biggest and the last representatives — in the whole world — of Anglo-Saxon "liberty", in the sense that they had no militarist cliques and bureaucracy, have completely sunk into the all-European filthy, bloody morass of bureaucratic-military institutions which subordinate everything to themselves, and suppress everything. Today, in Britain and America, too, "the precondition for every real people's revolution" is the smashing, the destruction of the "ready-made state machinery" (made and brought up to the "European", general imperialist, perfection in those countries in the years 1914-17).

其次，尤其应该注意马克思那句极其深刻的论断：摧毁官僚军事国家机器是“一切真正的人民革命的前提”。“人民革命”这个概念出自马克思之口，似乎有些奇怪，因此，那些自诩为马克思主义者的俄国普列汉诺夫派和孟什维克，以及斯特鲁维的追随者们，或许会认为这是马克思的“笔误”。他们已经把马克思主义扭曲成一种可悲的自由主义，以至于在他们眼中，除了资产阶级革命和无产阶级革命的对立之外，别无其他，甚至连这种对立本身，他们的解读也毫无生气。

Secondly, particular attention should be paid to Marx's extremely profound remark that the destruction of the bureaucratic-military state machine is "the precondition for every real people's revolution". This idea of a "people's revolution seems strange coming from Marx, so that the Russian Plekhanovites and Mensheviks, those followers of Struve who wish to be regarded as Marxists, might possibly declare such an expression to be a "slip of the pen" on Marx's part. They have reduced Marxism to such a state of wretchedly liberal distortion that nothing exists for them beyond the antithesis between bourgeois revolution and proletarian revolution, and even this antithesis they interpret in an utterly lifeless way.

如果我们以20世纪的革命为例，当然必须承认葡萄牙革命和土耳其革命都是资产阶级革命。然而，它们都不是“人民”革命，因为在这两场革命中，广大人民群众，也就是绝大多数民众，并没有积极主动地、独立地提出任何显著的经济和政治诉求。相比之下，尽管1905-1907年的俄国资产阶级革命不像葡萄牙革命和土耳其革命那样取得了“辉煌”的成就，但它无疑是一场“真正的人民”革命，因为广大人民群众，也就是绝大多数民众，以及那些遭受压迫和剥削的最底层社会群体，独立地站了起来，并在整个革命进程中留下了他们自身诉求的印记，他们试图以自己的方式建立一个新社会来取代正在被摧毁的旧社会。

If we take the revolutions of the 20th century as examples we shall, of course, have to admit that the Portuguese and the Turkish revolutions are both bourgeois revolutions. Neither of them, however, is a "people's" revolution, since in neither does the mass of the people, their vast majority, come out actively, independently, with their own economic and political demands to any noticeable degree. By contrast, although the Russian bourgeois revolution of 1905-07 displayed no such "brilliant" successes as at time fell to the Portuguese and Turkish revolutions, it was undoubtedly a "real people's" revolution, since the mass of the people, their majority, the very lowest social groups, crushed by oppression and exploitation, rose independently and stamped on the entire course of the revolution the imprint of their own demands, their attempt to build in their own way a new society in place of the old society that was being destroyed.

1871年的欧洲，无产阶级在任何一个国家都不占人口的大多数。一场真正能席卷大多数民众的“人民”革命，只有同时囊括无产阶级和农民，才能称之为“人民”革命。这两个阶级构成了“人民”。这两个阶级之所以团结在一起，是因为“官僚军事国家机器”压迫、镇压、剥削他们。摧毁、瓦解这个机器，才真正符合“人民”的利益，符合大多数人民、工人和大多数农民的利益，也是贫苦农民和无产阶级自由结盟的“前提条件”。没有这样的联盟，民主就不稳定，社会主义转型也无从谈起。

In Europe, in 1871, the proletariat did not constitute the majority of the people in any country on the Continent. A "people's" revolution, one actually sweeping the majority into its stream, could be such only if it embraced both the proletariat and the peasants. These two classes then constituted the "people". These two classes are united by the fact that the "bureaucratic-military state machine" oppresses, crushes, exploits them. To smash this machine, to break it up, is truly in the interest of the "people", of their majority, of the workers and most of the peasants, is "the precondition" for a free alliance of the poor peasant and the proletarians, whereas without such an alliance democracy is unstable and socialist transformation is impossible.

众所周知，巴黎公社实际上正在努力达成这样的联盟，尽管由于内部和外部的诸多原因，它未能实现这一目标。

As is well known, the Paris Commune was actually working its way toward such an alliance, although it did not reach its goal owing to a number of circumstances, internal and external.

因此，马克思在谈到“真正的人民革命”时，丝毫没有忽视小资产阶级的特殊性（他对此着墨颇多），而是严格考虑了1871年欧洲大陆大多数国家阶级力量的实际平衡。另一方面，他指出，为了工人和农民的共同利益，必须“摧毁”国家机器，因为这能将他们团结起来，并让他们共同承担清除“寄生虫”并用新事物取而代之的任务。

Consequently, in speaking of a "real people's revolution", Marx, without in the least discounting the special features of the petty bourgeois (he spoke a great deal about them and often), took strict account of the actual balance of class forces in most of the continental countries of Europe in 1871. On the other hand, he stated that the "smashing" of the state machine was required by the interests of both the workers and the peasants, that it united them, that it placed before them the common task of removing the "parasite" and of replacing it by something new.

具体通过什么方式？

By what exactly?





 





 

2. 什么可以替代损坏的状态机？

2. What is to Replace the Smashed State Machine?

1847年，马克思在《共产党宣言》中对这个问题的回答还纯粹是抽象的；确切地说，他的回答指出了任务，但没有指出完成任务的方法。《共产党宣言》给出的答案是，这台机器将被“组织起来的无产阶级作为统治阶级”所取代，这要通过“民主斗争的胜利”来实现。

In 1847, in the Communist Manifesto, Marx's answer to this question was as yet a purely abstract one; to be exact, it was an answer that indicated he tasks, but not the ways of accomplishing them. The answer given in the Communist Manifesto was that this machine was to be replaced by "the proletariat organized as the ruling class", by the "winning of the battle of democracy".

马克思不沉迷于乌托邦；他期望群众运动的经验能够回答以下问题：无产阶级作为统治阶级的组织将采取何种具体形式，以及这种组织将以何种方式与最彻底、最一致的“民主斗争的胜利”相结合。

Marx did not indulge in utopias; he expected the experience of the mass movement to provide the reply to the question as to the specific forms this organisation of the proletariat as the ruling class would assume and as to the exact manner in which this organisation would be combined with the most complete, most consistent "winning of the battle of democracy."

尽管巴黎公社的经验十分有限，但马克思在《法兰西内战》一书中对其进行了极其细致的分析。让我们引用这部著作中最重要的一些段落。[本章以下所有引文，除一处外，均如此标注——编者注]

Marx subjected the experience of the Commune, meagre as it was, to the most careful analysis in The Civil War in France. Let us quote the most important passages of this work. [All the following quotes in this Chapter, with one exception, are so citied - Ed.]

源于中世纪，并在19世纪发展成为“中央集权的国家权力，其机构涵盖无处不在的常备军、警察、官僚机构、宗教机构和司法机构”。随着资本与劳动阶级对抗的加剧，“国家权力日益呈现出为镇压工人阶级而组织的公共力量、阶级统治机器的性质。每一次标志着阶级斗争进展的革命之后，国家权力的纯粹强制性质都愈发凸显。”1848-49年革命后，国家权力沦为“资本对抗劳动的民族战争工具”。第二帝国巩固了这一局面。

Originating from the Middle Ages, there developed in the 19th century "the centralized state power, with its ubiquitous organs of standing army, police, bureaucracy, clergy, and judicature." With the development of class antagonisms between capital and labor, "state power assumed more and more the character of a public force organized for the suppression of the working class, of a machine of class rule. After every revolution, which marks an advance in the class struggle, the purely coercive character of the state power stands out in bolder and bolder relief." After the revolution of 1848-49, state power became "the national war instruments of capital against labor". The Second Empire consolidated this.

“公社是帝国的直接对立面。”它是“一种共和国的具体形式，它不仅要消除君主制的阶级统治形式，还要消除阶级统治本身。”

"The direct antithesis to the empire was the Commune." It was the "specific form" of "a republic that was not only to remove the monarchical form of class rule, but class rule itself."

这种“具体”的无产阶级社会主义共和国形式是什么？它开始建立的国家是什么样的？

What was this "specific" form of the proletarian, socialist republic? What was the state it began to create?

“因此，公社的第一项法令就是解散常备军，代之以武装人民。”

"The first decree of the Commune, therefore, was the suppression of the standing army, and the substitution for it of the armed people."

现在，所有自称社会主义政党的政党的纲领中都包含了这一诉求。然而，真正体现他们纲领价值的，是我们的社会革命党人和孟什维克的行为：他们在二月二十七日革命后，立即拒绝执行这一诉求！

This demand now figures in the programme of every party calling itself socialist. The real worth of their programme, however, is best shown by the behavior of our Social-Revolutionists and mensheviks, who, right after the revolution of February 27, refused to carry out this demand!

“公社由市政议员组成，这些议员由城镇各选区的普选产生，他们负责且随时可被撤换。公社成员大多是工人，或是公认的工人阶级代表……此前作为政府工具的警察，立即被剥夺了政治属性，成为公社负责且随时可被撤换的代理人。所有其他行政部门的官员也是如此。从公社成员到普通民众，公共服务都必须按工人的工资标准进行。国家高级官员的特权和代表津贴随着他们自身的消失而消失……公社在废除了常备军和警察——旧政府的武力工具——之后，立即着手摧毁精神压迫的工具——神职人员的权力……司法官员失去了虚假的独立性……从此以后，他们必须是选举产生的、负责的，并且……”可撤销的。

"The Commune was formed of the municipal councillors, chosen by universal suffrage in the various wards of the town, responsible and revocable at any time. The majority of its members were naturally working men, or acknowledged representatives of the working class.... The police, which until then had been the instrument of the Government, was at once stripped of its political attributes, and turned into the responsible, and at all times revocable, agent of the Commune. So were the officials of all other branches of the administration. From the members of the Commune downwards, the public service had to be done at workmen's wages. The privileges and the representation allowances of the high dignitaries of state disappeared along with the high dignitaries themselves.... Having once got rid of the standing army and the police, the instruments of physical force of the old government, the Commune proceeded at once to break the instrument of spiritual suppression, the power of the priests.... The judicial functionaries lost that sham independence... they were thenceforward to be elective, responsible, and revocable."

因此，公社表面上似乎只是以更充分的民主取代了被摧毁的国家机器：废除常备军；所有官员均由选举产生并可被罢免。但事实上，这种“仅仅”意味着某些制度被其他本质上不同的制度所彻底取代。这正是“量变质”的典型例子：民主制度以尽可能充分和一致的方式引入，从资产阶级民主转变为无产阶级民主；国家（即镇压特定阶级的特殊力量）转变为某种不再是国家本身的东西。

The Commune, therefore, appears to have replaced the smashed state machine "only" by fuller democracy: abolition of the standing army; all officials to be elected and subject to recall. But as a matter of fact this "only" signifies a gigantic replacement of certain institutions by other institutions of a fundamentally different type. This is exactly a case of "quantity being transformed into quality": democracy, introduced as fully and consistently as is at all conceivable, is transformed from bourgeois into proletarian democracy; from the state (= a special force for the suppression of a particular class) into something which is no longer the state proper.

镇压资产阶级、粉碎其抵抗仍然是必要的。这对巴黎公社来说尤其如此；而公社失败的原因之一，正是它在这方面不够坚定。然而，镇压的机构在这里是大多数民众，而不是像奴隶制、农奴制和雇佣奴隶制下那样的少数人。既然大多数民众自己就能镇压压迫者，那么就不再需要专门的镇压部队了！从这个意义上讲，国家开始衰落。不再需要特权少数人的特殊机构（特权官员、常备军首领），大多数民众可以直接履行所有这些职能；而且，国家权力的职能越是由全体人民行使的，国家权力存在的必要性就越低。

It is still necessary to suppress the bourgeoisie and crush their resistance. This was particularly necessary for the Commune; and one of the reasons for its defeat was that it did not do this with sufficient determination. The organ of suppression, however, is here the majority of the population, and not a minority, as was always the case under slavery, serfdom, and wage slavery. And since the majority of people itself suppresses its oppressors, a 'special force" for suppression is no longer necessary! In this sense, the state begins to wither away. Instead of the special institutions of a privileged minority (privileged officialdom, the chiefs of the standing army), the majority itself can directly fulfil all these functions, and the more the functions of state power are performed by the people as a whole, the less need there is for the existence of this power.

就此而言，马克思强调的公社的以下措施尤为值得注意：废除一切代表津贴和官员的一切金钱特权，将所有国家公务员的报酬降至“工人工资”水平。这比任何其他事物都更清楚地表明了从资产阶级民主向无产阶级民主的转变，从压迫者的民主向被压迫阶级的民主的转变，从国家作为镇压特定阶级的“特殊力量”向依靠人民大多数——工人和农民——的普遍力量镇压压迫者的转变。而正是在这个尤为突出、或许是国家问题上最重要的方面，马克思的思想却被彻底忽视了！在数量众多的通俗评论中，这一点只字未提。采取的做法是对此保持沉默，仿佛这是一种过时的“天真”，就像基督徒在他们的宗教被赋予国教地位后，“忘记”了早期基督教的“天真”及其民主革命精神一样。

In this connection, the following measures of the Commune, emphasized by Marx, are particularly noteworthy: the abolition of all representation allowances, and of all monetary privileges to officials, the reduction of the remuneration of all servants of the state to the level of "workmen's wages". This shows more clearly than anything else the turn from bourgeois to proletarian democracy, from the democracy of the oppressors to that of the oppressed classes, from the state as a "special force" for the suppression of a particular class to the suppression of the oppressors by the general force of the majority of the people - the workers and the peasants. And it is on this particularly striking point, perhaps the most important as far as the problem of the state is concerned, that the ideas of Marx have been most completely ignored! In popular commentaries, the number of which is legion, this is not mentioned. The thing done is to keep silent about it as if it were a piece of old-fashioned "naivete", just as Christians, after their religion had been given the status of state religion, "forgot" the "naivete" of primitive Christianity with its democratic revolutionary spirit.

削减高级官员的薪酬似乎“仅仅”是天真、原始的民主的要求。现代机会主义的“创始人”之一，前社会民主党人爱德华·伯恩斯坦，曾多次重复资产阶级对“原始”民主的粗俗嘲讽。像所有机会主义者，以及现在的考茨基主义者一样，他完全不明白，首先，从资本主义向社会主义的过渡离不开某种程度的“回归”到“原始”民主（否则，多数人，乃至全体民众，又如何履行国家职能呢？）；其次，基于资本主义和资本主义文化的“原始民主”与史前或前资本主义时代的原始民主截然不同。资本主义文化创造了大规模生产、工厂、铁路、邮政服务、电话等等，在此基础上，旧“国家权力”的绝大多数职能都变得如此简单，可以简化为登记、归档和核查等极其简单的操作，以至于每个识字的人都能轻松完成，而且完全可以用普通“工人的工资”来完成，这些职能可以（而且必须）被剥夺一切特权和一切“官方威严”的表象。

The reduction of the remuneration of high state officials seem "simply" a demand of naive, primitive democracy. One of the "founders" of modern opportunism, the ex-Social-Democrat Eduard Bernstein, has more than once repeated the vulgar bourgeois jeers at "primitive" democracy. Like all opportunists, and like the present Kautskyites, he did not understand at all that, first of all, the transition from capitalism to socialism is impossible without a certain "reversion" to "primitive" democracy (for how else can the majority, and then the whole population without exception, proceed to discharge state functions?); and that, secondly, "primitive democracy" based on capitalism and capitalist culture is not the same as primitive democracy in prehistoric or precapitalist times. Capitalist culture has created large-scale production, factories, railways, the postal service, telephones, etc., and on this basis the great majority of the functions of the old "state power" have become so simplified and can be reduced to such exceedingly simple operations of registration, filing, and checking that they can be easily performed by every literate person, can quite easily be performed for ordinary "workmen's wages", and that these functions can (and must) be stripped of every shadow of privilege, of every semblance of "official grandeur".

所有官员，无一例外，均由选举产生，并随时可被罢免；他们的薪俸降至普通“工人工资”水平——这些简单而“不言而喻”的民主措施，在完全统一工人阶级和大多数农民利益的同时，也成为从资本主义向社会主义过渡的桥梁。这些措施涉及国家重组，纯粹是社会的政治重组；但当然，只有与已经完成或正在筹备的“剥夺者”的剥夺联系起来，即与资本主义生产资料私有制向社会所有制的转变联系起来，这些措施才能获得其全部意义和重要性。

All officials, without exception, elected and subject to recall at any time, their salaries reduced to the level of ordinary "workmen's wages" — these simple and "self-evident" democratic measures, while completely uniting the interests of the workers and the majority of the peasants, at the same time serve as a bridge leading from capitalism to socialism. These measures concern the reorganization of the state, the purely political reorganization of society; but, of course, they acquire their full meaning and significance only in connection with the "expropriation of the expropriators" either bring accomplished or in preparation, i.e., with the transformation of capitalist private ownership of the means of production into social ownership.

马克思写道：“公社通过废除两大开支来源——军队和官僚机构，使一切资产阶级革命的口号——廉价政府——成为现实。”

"The Commune," Marx wrote, "made the catchword of all bourgeois revolutions, cheap government, a reality, by abolishing the two greatest sources of expenditure - the army and the officialdom."

如同其他小资产阶级阶层一样，农民中只有极少数人能够“飞黄腾达”，以资产阶级的方式“出人头地”，即成为富裕的资产阶级，或身居要职、享有特权。在每一个有农民的资本主义国家（大多数资本主义国家都有农民），绝大多数农民都受到政府的压迫，渴望推翻政府，渴望建立一个“廉价”的政府。这只有无产阶级才能实现；而无产阶级实现这一目标的同时，也朝着国家的社会主义改造迈出了一步。

From the peasants, as from other sections of the petty bourgeoisie, only an insignificant few "rise to the top", "get on in the world" in the bourgeois sense, i.e., become either ell-to-do, bourgeois, or officials in secure and privileged positions. In every capitalist country where there are peasants (as there are in most capitalist countries), the vast majority of them are oppressed by the government and long for its overthrow, long for "cheap" government. This can be achieved only by the proletariat; and by achieving it, the proletariat at the same time takes a step towards the socialist reorganization of the state.



 



 

3.废除议会制

3. Abolition of Parliamentarism

马克思写道：“公社将是一个工作机构，而不是议会机构，它将同时具有行政和立法职能……”

"The Commune," Marx wrote, "was to be a working, not a parliamentary, body, executive and legislative at the same time....

“与其每三到六年决定由统治阶级的哪位成员代表人民在议会中镇压人民，不如实行普选，让人民在公社中组成，就像个人选举权让每个雇主都能为自己的企业寻找工人、工头和会计一样。”

"Instead of deciding once in three or six years which member of the ruling class was to represent and repress [ver- and zertreten] the people in parliament, universal suffrage was to serve the people constituted in communes, as individual suffrage serves every other employer in the search for workers, foremen and accountants for his business."

由于社会沙文主义和机会主义的盛行，1871年对议会制度的这一卓越批判如今也沦为马克思主义“被遗忘的话语”。那些职业化的内阁部长和议员，那些背叛无产阶级的“实用主义”社会主义者，将对议会制度的批判全部留给了无政府主义者，并以此为由，将所有对议会制度的批判都斥为“无政府主义”！毫不奇怪，“先进”议会国家的无产阶级对谢德曼、戴维、莱吉恩、森巴特、雷诺德尔、亨德森、范德维尔德、斯陶宁、布兰廷、比索拉蒂斯等人这样的“社会主义者”感到厌恶，因此越来越频繁地同情无政府工团主义，尽管后者只不过是机会主义的孪生兄弟。

Owing to the prevalence of social-chauvinism and opportunism, this remarkable criticism of parliamentarism, made in 1871, also belongs now to the "forgotten words" of Marxism. The professional Cabinet Ministers and parliamentarians, the traitors to the proletariat and the "practical" socialists of our day, have left all criticism of parliamentarism to the anarchists, and, on this wonderfully reasonable ground, they denounce all criticism of parliamentarism as "anarchism"!! It is not surprising that the proletariat of the "advanced" parliamentary countries, disgusted with such "socialists" as the Scheidemanns, Davids, Legiens, Sembats, Renaudels, Hendersons, Vanderveldes, Staunings, Brantings, Bissolatis, and Co., has been with increasing frequency giving its sympathies to anarcho-syndicalism, in spite of the fact that the latter is merely the twin brother of opportunism.

然而，对马克思而言，革命辩证法绝非普列汉诺夫、考茨基等人所将其曲解为的空洞时髦的口号、玩具拨浪鼓。马克思深知如何无情地批判无政府主义，因为它甚至无法利用资产阶级议会制度这“猪圈”，尤其是在形势明显不具备革命性的情况下；但与此同时，他也懂得如何对议会制度进行真正革命性的无产阶级批判。

For Marx, however, revolutionary dialectics was never the empty fashionable phrase, the toy rattle, which Plekhanov, Kautsky and others have made of it. Marx knew how to break with anarchism ruthlessly for its inability to make use even of the "pigsty" of bourgeois parliamentarism, especially when the situation was obviously not revolutionary; but at the same time he knew how to subject parliamentarism to genuinely revolutionary proletarian criticism.

每隔几年通过议会决定由统治阶级的哪些成员来镇压和摧毁人民——这才是资产阶级议会制的真正本质，不仅在议会立宪君主制国家，而且在最民主的共和国也是如此。

To decide once every few years which members of the ruling class is to repress and crush the people through parliament - this is the real essence of bourgeois parliamentarism, not only in parliamentary- constitutional monarchies, but also in the most democratic republics.

但是，如果我们讨论国家问题，如果我们把议会制度视为国家制度之一，从无产阶级在这一领域的任务角度来看，摆脱议会制度的出路是什么？如何才能抛弃它？

But if we deal with the question of the state, and if we consider parliamentarism as one of the institutions of the state, from the point of view of the tasks of the proletariat in this field, what is the way out of parliamentarism? How can it be dispensed with?

我们必须再次指出：马克思基于对巴黎公社的研究而得出的教训已被彻底遗忘，以至于当今的“社会民主主义者”（即当今社会主义的叛徒）除了无政府主义或反动主义的批评之外，根本无法理解对议会制度的任何批评。

Once again, we must say: the lessons of Marx, based on the study of the Commune, have been so completely forgotten that the present-day "Social-Democrat" (i.e., present-day traitor to socialism) really cannot understand any criticism of parliamentarism other than anarchist or reactionary criticism.

当然，摆脱议会制的出路并非废除代表机构和选举原则，而是将代表机构从空谈机构转变为“实干”机构。“公社本应是一个实干机构，而非议会机构，它既是行政机构，又是立法机构。”

The way out of parliamentarism is not, of course, the abolition of representative institutions and the elective principle, but the conversion of the representative institutions from talking shops into "working" bodies. "The Commune was to be a working, not a parliamentary, body, executive and legislative at the same time."

“一个运作机构，而非议会机构”——这番话直击当今议会制国家的要害，从美国到瑞士，从法国到英国，再到挪威等等——在这些国家，真正的“国家”事务都在幕后进行，由各部门、总理府和总参谋部负责。议会沦为空谈的工具，其唯一目的就是愚弄“普通民众”。即便在俄罗斯这个资产阶级民主共和国，议会制的种种弊端也立刻显露出来，甚至在它还没来得及建立起一个真正的议会之前就已如此。像斯科别列夫、采列捷利、切尔诺夫和阿夫克森季耶夫这样的庸俗庸俗主义的代表人物，甚至成功地以最令人作呕的资产阶级议会制的方式污染了苏维埃，将其变成了空谈的场所。在苏维埃，那些“社会主义”部长们用花言巧语和决议愚弄着轻信的乡下人。政府内部也进行着某种永无休止的改组，一方面是为了让尽可能多的社会革命党人和孟什维克能够轮流接近“蛋糕”，也就是那些高薪而体面的职位；另一方面是为了“吸引”人民的“注意力”。与此同时，各部委和军队参谋部则在“处理”着“国家”事务。

"A working, not a parliamentary body" - this is a blow straight from the shoulder at the present-day parliamentarian country, from America to Switzerland, from France to Britain, Norway and so forth - in these countries the real business of "state" is performed behind the scenes and is carried on by the departments, chancelleries, and General Staffs. parliament is given up to talk for the special purpose of fooling the "common people". This is so true that even in the Russian republic, a bourgeois-democratic republic, all these sins of parliamentarism came out at once, even before it managed to set up a real parliament. The heroes of rotten philistinism, such as the skobelevs and tseretelis, the Chernovs and Avksentyevs, have even succeeded in polluting the Soviets after the fashion of the most disgusting bourgeois parliamentarism, in converting them into mere talking shops. In the Soviets, the "socialist" Ministers are fooling the credulous rustics with phrase-mongering and resolutions. In the government itself a sort of permanent shuffle is going on in order that, on the one hand, as many Socialist-Revolutionaries and Mensheviks as possible may in turn get near the "pie", the lucrative and honorable posts, and that, on the other hand, the "attention" of the people may be "engaged". meanwhile the chancelleries and army staffs "do" the business of "state".

执政的社会革命党机关报《人民报》最近在一篇社论中——以“上流社会”人士无可比拟的坦率（在这个社会里，“所有人”都参与了政治卖淫）——承认，即使在由“社会主义者”（请注意这个标记！）领导的部委里，整个官僚机构实际上也未曾改变，依然沿用旧有的运作方式，并且肆无忌惮地破坏革命措施！即使没有这一承认，社会革命党人和孟什维克参与政府的实际历史难道还不足以证明这一点吗？然而值得注意的是，在立宪民主党人的圈子里，切尔诺夫、鲁萨诺夫、岑济诺夫以及《人民报》的其他编辑们已经完全丧失了羞耻心，竟然厚颜无耻地宣称，在“他们”的部委里，一切都没有改变！用革命民主的口号来愚弄农村的淳朴民众，用官僚主义和繁文缛节来“取悦”资本家——这就是“诚实”联盟的本质。

Dyelo Naroda, the organ of the ruling Socialist-Revolutionary Party, recently admitted in a leading article - with the matchless frankness of people of "good society", in which "all" are engaged in political prostitution - that even in the ministeries headed by the "socialists" (save the mark!), the whole bureaucratic apparatus is in fact unchanged, is working in the old way and quite "freely" sabotaging revolutionary measures! Even without this admission, does not the actual history of the participation of the Socialist-Revolutionaries and Mensheviks in the government prove this? It is noteworthy, however, that in the ministerial company of the Cadets, the Chernovs, Rusanovs, Zenzinovs, and other editors of Dyelo Naroda have so completely lost all sense of shame as to brazenly assert, as if it were a mere bagetelle, that in "their" ministeries everything is unchanged!! Revolutionary-democratic phrases to gull the rural Simple Simons, and bureaucracy and red tape to "gladden the hearts" of the capitalists - that is the essence of the "honest" coalition.

公社以腐败堕落的资产阶级社会机构中的议会制度取而代之，在这种制度下，言论自由和讨论不会沦为欺骗，因为议员们必须亲自工作，必须执行自己制定的法律，必须亲自检验实际取得的成果，并直接向选民负责。代议制机构依然存在，但这里不存在作为一种特殊制度的议会制度，不存在立法和行政之间的分工，也不存在代表享有的特权地位。我们不能想象没有代议制机构的民主，即使是无产阶级民主，但我们能够也必须想象没有议会制度的民主，如果对我们而言，对资产阶级社会的批判不仅仅是空谈，如果推翻资产阶级统治的愿望是我们真挚的愿望，而不是像孟什维克、社会革命党人、谢德曼、莱吉恩、斯布拉特和范德维尔德之流那样，仅仅是为了拉拢工人选票而发出的“选举”口号。

The Commune substitutes for the venal and rotten parliamentarism of bourgeois society institutions in which freedom of opinion and discussion does not degenerate into deception, for the parliamentarians themselves have to work, have to execute their own laws, have themselves to test the results achieved in reality, and to account directly to their constituents. Representative institutions remain, but there is no parliamentarism here as a special system, as the division of labor between the legislative and the executive, as a privileged position for the deputies. We cannot imagine democracy, even proletarian democracy, without representative institutions, but we can and must imagine democracy without parliamentarism, if criticism of bourgeois society is not mere words for us, if the desire to overthrow the rule of the bourgeoisie is our earnest and sincere desire, and not a mere "election" cry for catching workers' votes, as it is with the Mensheviks and Socialist-Revolutionaries, and also the Scheidemanns and Legiens, the Smblats and Vanderveldes.

值得注意的是，马克思在谈到公社和无产阶级民主所必需的官员的职能时，将他们与“其他所有雇主”的工人，即普通资本主义企业的工人，以及其“工人、工头和会计”进行了比较。

It is extremely instructive to note that, in speaking of the function of those officials who are necessary for the Commune and for proletarian democracy, Marx compares them to the workers of "every other employer", that is, of the ordinary capitalist enterprise, with its "workers, foremen, and accountants".

马克思的思想中丝毫没有乌托邦主义的痕迹，他并没有虚构或发明一个“新”社会。相反，他研究的是新社会从旧社会中诞生的过程，以及从旧社会向新社会过渡的各种形式，将其视为一场群众性的无产阶级运动，并试图从中汲取实践经验。他从巴黎公社“学习”，正如所有伟大的革命思想家都毫不犹豫地从被压迫阶级的伟大运动经验中学习一样，他从未用迂腐的“说教”（例如普列汉诺夫的“他们不应该拿起武器”或采列捷利的“一个阶级必须自我限制”）来对待这些运动。

There is no trace of utopianism in Marx, in the sense that he made up or invented a "new" society. No, he studied the birth of the new society out of the old, and the forms of transition from the latter to the former, as a mass proletarian movement and tried to draw practical lessons from it. He "Learned" from the Commune, just as all the great revolutionary thinkers learned unhesitatingly from the experience of great movements of the oppressed classes, and never addressed them with pedantic "homilies" (such as Plekhanov's: "They should not have taken up arms" or Tsereteli's: "A class must limit itself").

一下子在所有地方彻底废除官僚机构是不可能的，那是乌托邦。但是，立刻摧毁旧的官僚机器，并立即开始建设一个新的机器，以便逐步废除所有官僚机构——这不是乌托邦，这是巴黎公社的经验，是革命无产阶级的直接和紧迫的任务。

Abolishing the bureaucracy at once, everywhere and completely, is out of the question. It is a utopia. But to smash the old bureaucratic machine at once and to begin immediately to construct a new one that will make possible the gradual abolition of all bureaucracy - this is not a utopia, it is the experience of the Commune, the direct and immediate task of the revolutionary proletariat.

资本主义简化了“国家”行政职能；它使得抛弃“老板”成为可能，并将整个事情限制在无产阶级（作为统治阶级）的组织之内，无产阶级将以整个社会的名义雇用“工人、工头和会计”。

Capitalism simplifies the functions of "state" administration; it makes it possible to cast "bossing" aside and to confine the whole matter to the organization of the proletarians (as the ruling class), which will hire "workers, foremen and accountants" in the name of the whole of society.

我们不是空想家，我们并不“梦想”一下子废除一切行政管理，废除一切服从。这些无政府主义的幻想，建立在对无产阶级专政任务的无知之上，与马克思主义完全背道而驰，事实上，它们只会把社会主义革命推迟到人民发生改变之后。不，我们希望在人民现在的状态下进行社会主义革命，在人民无法摆脱服从、控制和“工头和会计”的情况下进行革命。

We are not utopians, we do not "dream" of dispensing at once with all administration, with all subordination. These anarchist dreams, based upon incomprehension of the tasks of the proletarian dictatorship, are totally alien to Marxism, and, as a matter of fact, serve only to postpone the socialist revolution until people are different. No, we want the socialist revolution with people as they are now, with people who cannot dispense with subordination, control, and "foremen and accountants".

然而，这种服从必须是服从于所有被剥削劳动人民的武装先锋队，即无产阶级。必须立即着手，一夜之间，用“工头和会计”的简单职能取代国家官员的特定“领导”职能，这些职能普通城镇居民完全能够胜任，而且完全可以以“工人工资”来履行。

The subordination, however, must be to the armed vanguard of all the exploited and working people, i.e., to the proletariat. A beginning can and must be made at once, overnight, to replace the specific "bossing" of state officials by the simple functions of "foremen and accountants", functions which are already fully within the ability of the average town dweller and can well be performed for "workmen's wages".

我们工人阶级，要在资本主义已有的成果基础上，依靠我们自身的劳动经验，组织大规模生产，建立由武装工人国家政权支撑的铁腕纪律。我们要将国家官员的角色简化为仅仅执行我们指令的“工头和会计”（当然，还要借助各种各样、各种级别和各种技能的技术人员）。这就是我们的无产阶级任务，这就是我们能够也必须开始进行无产阶级革命的起点。这样的开端，建立在大规模生产的基础上，本身就将导致一切官僚机构的逐步“消亡”，逐步建立起一种秩序——一种不带引号的秩序，一种与雇佣奴隶制截然不同的秩序——在这种秩序下，控制和核算的职能将变得越来越简单，最终由每个人轮流履行，成为一种习惯，并最终不再是少数群体的专属职能。

We, the workers, shall organize large-scale production on the basis of what capitalism has already created, relying on our own experience as workers, establishing strict, iron discipline backed up by the state power of the armed workers. We shall reduce the role of state officials to that of simply carrying out our instructions as responsible, revocable, modestly paid "foremen and accountants" (of course, with the aid of technicians of all sorts, types and degrees). This is our proletarian task, this is what we can and must start with in accomplishing the proletarian revolution. Such a beginning, on the basis of large-scale production, will of itself lead to the gradual "withering away" of all bureaucracy, to the gradual creation of an order - an order without inverted commas, an order bearing no similarity to wage slavery - an order under which the functions of control and accounting, becoming more and more simple, will be performed by each in turn, will then become a habit and will finally die out as the special functions of a special section of the population.

上世纪七十年代一位机智的德国社会民主党人曾将邮政服务称为社会主义经济制度的典范。这话一点没错。如今，邮政服务是按照国家资本主义垄断模式组织的。帝国主义正逐步将所有托拉斯改造成类似的组织，在这些组织中，凌驾于过度劳累、忍饥挨饿的“普通”民众之上的，正是同样的资产阶级官僚机构。然而，社会管理机制已然存在。一旦我们推翻了资本家，用武装工人的铁腕镇压了这些剥削者的抵抗，摧毁了现代国家的官僚机器，我们将拥有一个装备精良、摆脱了“寄生虫”控制的机制，一个完全可以由团结起来的工人自己启动的机制。他们将雇佣技术人员、工头和会计，并像对待所有“国家”官员一样，向他们支付工人的工资。这是一个具体的、实际的任务，可以立即在所有信托机构中得到完成；完成这项任务将使劳动人民摆脱剥削；这项任务考虑到了公社已经开始实践的事情（尤其是在国家建设方面）。

A witty German Social-Democrat of the seventies of the last century called the postal service an example of the socialist economic system. This is very true. At the present the postal service is a business organized on the lines of state-capitalist monopoly. Imperialism is gradually transforming all trusts into organizations of a similar type, in which, standing over the "common" people, who are overworked and starved, one has the same bourgeois bureaucracy. But the mechanism of social management is here already to hand. Once we have overthrown the capitalists, crushed the resistance of these exploiters with the iron hand of the armed workers, and smashed the bureaucratic machinery of the modern state, we shall have a splendidly-equipped mechanism, freed from the "parasite", a mechanism which can very well be set going by the united workers themselves, who will hire technicians, foremen and accountants, and pay them all, as indeed all "state" officials in general, workmen's wages. Here is a concrete, practical task which can immediately be fulfilled in relation to all trusts, a task whose fulfilment will rid the working people of exploitation, a task which takes account of what the Commune had already begun to practice (particularly in building up the state).

按照邮政系统的模式组织整个经济，使技术人员、工头、会计以及所有官员的工资不得高于“工人的工资”，一切都在武装无产阶级的控制和领导之下——这就是我们眼下的目标。这将导致议会制度的废除和代议制机构的保留。这将使劳动阶级摆脱资产阶级对这些机构的剥削。

To organize the whole economy on the lines of the postal service so that the technicians, foremen and accountants, as well as all officials, shall receive salaries no higher than "a workman's wage", all under the control and leadership of the armed proletariat - that is our immediate aim. This is what will bring about the abolition of parliamentarism and the preservation of representative institutions. This is what will rid the laboring classes of the bourgeoisie's prostitution of these institutions.



 



 

4. 民族团结组织

4. Organisation of National Unity

在一份简要的国家组织纲要中（公社没有时间进一步发展），它明确指出，公社将成为哪怕是最小村庄的政治形式……各公社将在巴黎选举“国民代表大会”。

"In a brief sketch of national organization which the Commune had no time to develop, it states explicitly that the Commune was to be the political form of even the smallest village...." The communes were to elect the "National Delegation" in Paris.

“……中央政府仍然保留的少数但重要的职能，不会像之前故意歪曲的说法那样被压制，而是要转移到地方政府，即严格负责的官员手中。

"... The few but important functions which would still remain for a central government were not to to be suppressed, as had been deliberately mis-stated, but were to be transferred to communal, i.e., strictly responsible, officials.

“……民族团结不应被破坏，相反，应通过共同体宪法加以组织；民族团结应通过摧毁自诩为民族团结化身却妄图独立于民族、凌驾于民族之上的国家权力来实现，它不过是寄生于民族躯体上的赘生物。旧政府权力中那些仅具镇压作用的机构应被切除，而其合法职能则应从自诩凌驾于社会之上的权威手中夺回，并归还给那些对社会负责的公仆。”

"... National unity was not to be broken, but, on the contrary, organized by the communal constitution; it was to become a reality by the destruction of state power which posed as the embodiment of that unity yet wanted to be independent of, and superior to, the nation, on whose body it was but a parasitic excrescence. While the merely repressive organs of the old governmental power were to be amputated, its legitimate functions were to be wrested from an authority claiming the right to stand above society, and restored to the responsible servants of society."

当今社会民主党的机会主义者们未能理解——或许更准确地说，是拒绝理解——马克思的这些论述，这一点在叛逆的伯恩斯坦那本赫罗斯特拉特式的著作《社会主义的前提和社会民主党的任务》中体现得最为淋漓尽致。伯恩斯坦正是针对马克思的上述论述写道：

The extent to which the opportunists of present-day Social-Democracy have failed - perhaps it would be more true to say, have refused - to understand these observations of Marx is best shown by that book of Herostratean fame of the renegade Bernstein, The Premises of Socialism and the Tasks of the Social-Democrats. It is in connection with the above passage from Marx that Bernstein wrote that

“就其政治内容而言，”该纲领“在其所有基本特征上，都与蒲鲁东的联邦主义极为相似……尽管马克思与‘小资产阶级’蒲鲁东（伯恩斯坦特意将‘小资产阶级’一词加上引号，以示讽刺）在其他方面存在诸多分歧，但在这些方面，他们的论证思路却几乎完全一致。”伯恩斯坦继续说道，当然，市镇的重要性日益凸显，但“在我看来，民主的首要任务是否真的会像马克思和蒲鲁东所设想的那样，解散现代国家并彻底改造其组织结构（即由省议会和区议会的代表组成国民议会，而这些代表又由公社代表组成），从而导致原有的全国代表制模式消失，这一点值得怀疑。”

"as far as its political content", this programme "displays, in all its essential features, the greatest similarity to the federalism of Proudhon.... In spite of all the other points of difference between Marx and the 'petty-bourgeois' Proudhon [Bernstein places the word "petty-bourgeois" in inverted commas, to make it sound ironical] on these points, their lines of reasoning run as close as could be." Of course, Bernstein continues, the importance of the municipalities is growing, but "it seems doubtful to me whether the first job of democracy would be such a dissolution [Auflosung] of the modern states and such a complete transformation [Umwandlung] of their organization as is visualized by Marx and Proudhon (the formation of a National Assembly from delegates of the provincial of district assemblies, which, in their turn, would consist of delegates from the communes), so that consequently the previous mode of national representation would disappear."

（伯恩斯坦，《前提》，德文版，1899年，第134页和第136页）

(Bernstein, Premises, German edition, 1899, pp.134 and 136)

将马克思关于“摧毁国家政权——一个寄生性的赘生物”的观点与蒲鲁东的联邦制混为一谈，简直是荒谬至极！但这并非偶然，因为机会主义者根本不会想到，马克思在这里根本不是在谈论与中央集权相对的联邦制，而是在谈论摧毁存在于所有资产阶级国家的旧的资产阶级国家机器。

To confuse Marx's view on the "destruction of state power, a parasitic excrescence", with Proudhon's federalism is positively monstrous! But it is no accident, for it never occurs to the opportunist that Marx does not speak here at all about federalism as opposed to centralism, but about smashing the old, bourgeois state machine which exists in all bourgeois countries.

机会主义者唯一能想到的，就是他周围所看到的，在小资产阶级庸俗主义和“改良主义者”停滞不前的环境中，那就是只有“市政当局”！机会主义者甚至已经丧失了思考无产阶级革命的习惯。

The only thing that does occur to the opportunist is what he sees around him, in an environment of petty-bourgeois philistinism and "reformists" stagnation, namely, only "municipalities"! The opportunist has even grown out of the habit of thinking about proletarian revolution.

这简直荒谬至极。但令人惊讶的是，竟然没有人就这一点与伯恩斯坦争论。伯恩斯坦的观点遭到了许多人的反驳，尤其是在俄罗斯文学界的普列汉诺夫和欧洲文学界的考茨基，但他们两人都未曾提及伯恩斯坦对马克思的这种歪曲。

It is ridiculous. But the remarkable thing is that nobody argued with Bernstein on this point. Bernstein has been refuted by many, especially by Plekhanov in Russian literature and by Kautsky in European literature, but neither of them has said anything about this distortion of Marx by Bernstein.

机会主义者早已忘记了如何进行革命思考，如何专注于革命本身，以至于他们把“联邦制”归于马克思，并将马克思与无政府主义创始人蒲鲁东混淆。至于自称正统马克思主义者和革命马克思主义理论捍卫者的考茨基和普列汉诺夫，他们对此却保持沉默！这正是考茨基主义者和机会主义者在马克思主义与无政府主义的区别问题上，导致观点极端庸俗化的根源之一，我们将在后文中再次讨论这个问题。

The opportunist has so much forgotten how to think in a revolutionary way and to dwell on revolution that he attributes "federalism" to Marx, whom he confuses with the founder of anarchism, Proudhon. As for Kautsky and Plekhanov, who claim to be orthodox Marxists and defenders of the theory of revolutionary Marxism, they are silent on this point! Here is one of the roots of the extreme vulgarization of the views on the difference between Marxism and anarchism, which is characteristic of both the Kautskyites and the opportunists, and which we shall discuss again later.

在马克思上述关于巴黎公社经验的论述中，丝毫没有联邦主义的痕迹。马克思在这一点上与蒲鲁东的观点一致，而机会主义者伯恩斯坦却对此视而不见。马克思在这一点上与蒲鲁东的观点恰恰相反，而伯恩斯坦却认为他们之间存在相似之处。

There is not a trace of federalism in Marx's above-quoted observation on the experience of the Commune. Marx agreed with Proudhon on the very point that the opportunist Bernstein did not see. Marx disagreed with Proudhon on the very point on which Bernstein found a similarity between them.

马克思与普鲁东的观点一致，他们都主张“摧毁”现代国家机器。无论是机会主义者还是考茨基主义者，都不愿承认马克思主义与无政府主义（包括普鲁东和巴枯宁）在这一问题上的观点相似，因为这正是他们与马克思主义的分歧所在。

Marx agreed with Proudhon in that they both stood for the "smashing" of the modern state machine. Neither the opportunists nor the Kautskyites wish to see the similarity of views on this point between Marxism and anarchism (both Proudhon and Bakunin) because this is where they have departed from Marxism.

马克思与蒲鲁东和巴枯宁的分歧恰恰在于联邦制问题（更不用说无产阶级专政了）。联邦制原则是小资产阶级无政府主义观点的必然结果。马克思是中央集权主义者。他刚才引述的论述丝毫没有背离中央集权主义。只有那些对国家抱有庸俗“迷信”的人才会把摧毁资产阶级国家机器误认为摧毁中央集权主义！

Marx disagreed both with Proudhon and Bakunin precisely on the question of federalism (not to mention the dictatorship of the proletariat). Federalism as a principle follows logically from the petty-bourgeois views of anarchism. Marx was a centralist. There is no departure whatever from centralism in his observations just quoted. Only those who are imbued with the philistine "superstitious belief" in the state can mistake the destruction of the bourgeois state machine for the destruction of centralism!

如果无产阶级和贫苦农民掌握了国家政权，自由地组织起来成立公社，联合所有公社的行动，打击资本家，镇压资本家的抵抗，将私有的铁路、工厂、土地等等全部归于全国人民，归于整个社会，这难道不是中央集权吗？这难道不是最彻底的民主中央集权，而且是无产阶级中央集权吗？

Now if the proletariat and the poor peasants take state power into their own hands, organize themselves quite freely in communes, and unite the action of all the communes in striking at capital, in crushing the resistance of the capitalists, and in transferring the privately-owned railways, factories, land and so on to the entire nation, to the whole of society, won't that be centralism? Won't that be the most consistent democratic centralism and, moreover, proletarian centralism?

伯恩斯坦根本无法想象自愿集中制的可能性，也无法想象无产阶级公社为了摧毁资产阶级统治和资产阶级国家机器而自愿融合的可能性。像所有庸俗之辈一样，伯恩斯坦把集中制想象成一种只能自上而下强加和维持的东西，只能由官僚机构和军阀集团来维持。

Bernstein simply cannot conceive of the possibility of voluntary centralism, of the voluntary fusion of the proletarian communes, for the sole purpose of destroying bourgeois rule and the bourgeois state machine. Like all philistines, Bernstein pictures centralism as something which can be imposed and maintained solely from above, and solely by the bureaucracy and military clique.

仿佛预见到自己的观点可能会被曲解，马克思明确强调，所谓公社想要破坏民族统一、废除中央政权的指控是蓄意捏造的谎言。马克思特意使用了“民族统一……是要组织起来的”这句话，以此来表明自觉的、民主的、无产阶级的中央集权与资产阶级的、军事的、官僚的中央集权之间的区别。

As though foreseeing that his views might be distorted, Marx expressly emphasized that the charge that the Commune had wanted to destroy national unity, to abolish the central authority, was a deliberate fraud. Marx purposely used the words: "National unity was... to be organized", so as to oppose conscious, democratic, proletarian centralism to bourgeois, military, bureaucratic centralism.

但最聋的莫过于那些充耳不闻的人。而当今社会民主党的机会主义者最不愿听到的，正是摧毁国家政权、切除寄生虫般的赘生物。

But there are none so deaf as those who will not hear. And the very thing the opportunists of present-day Social-Democracy do not want to hear about it the destruction of state power, the amputation of the parasitic excrescence.



 



 

5. 废除寄生国家

5. Aboloition of the Parasite State

我们已经引用了马克思关于这个问题的言论，现在我们必须对其进行补充。

We have already quoted Marx's words on the subject, and we must now supplement them.

他写道：“新出现的历史产物通常难逃这样的命运：它们会被误认为是某种更古老甚至已经消亡的社会生活形式的对应物，因为它们可能与这些旧形式有某种相似之处。因此，这个打破现代国家权力的新公社，被视为中世纪公社的复兴……被视为小国联盟（正如孟德斯鸠和吉伦特派所设想的那样）……被视为反对过度集权的旧斗争的夸张形式……”

"It is generally the fate of new historical creations," he wrote, "to be mistaken for the counterpart of older and even defunct forms of social life, to which they may bear a certain likeness. Thus, this new Commune, which breaks [bricht, smashes] the modern state power, has been regarded as a revival of the medieval communes... as a federation of small states (as Montesquieu and the Girondins visualized it)... as an exaggerated form of the old struggle against overcentralization....

“……《共同体宪法》本可将此前被‘国家’这个寄生虫般的赘生物所吸收的所有力量归还给社会肌体，这个赘生物一直以来都在蚕食和阻碍社会的自由流动。仅凭这一举措，它就能开启法国的复兴……”

"... The Communal Constitution would have restored to the social body all the forces hitherto absorbed by that parasitic excrescence, the 'state', feeding upon and hampering the free movement of society. By this one act it would have initiated the regeneration of France....

“……公社宪法本应使农村生产者处于其所在地区中心城镇的思想领导之下，并在那里确保城镇工人成为他们利益的天然受托人。公社的存在本身自然包含地方自治，但这种自治不再是制衡国家权力的手段，如今已变得多余。”

"... The Communal Constitution would have brought the rural producers under the intellectual lead of the central towns of their districts, and there secured to them, in the town working men, the natural trustees of their interests. The very existence of the Commune involved, as a matter of course, local self-government, but no longer as a counterpoise to state power, now become superfluous."

“打破国家政权”，将其视为“寄生赘生物”；“截肢”，“粉碎”；“国家政权，现在变得多余了”——这些都是马克思在评价和分析巴黎公社的经验时，用来指代国家的表述。

"Breaking state power", which as a "parasitic excrescence"; its "amputation", its "smashing"; "state power, now become superfluous" - these are the expressions Marx used in regard to the state when appraising and analyzing the experience of the Commune.

所有这些著作写于不到半个世纪前；如今，我们却不得不进行一番如同挖掘般的工作，才能将未经歪曲的马克思主义带给广大人民群众。马克思亲历的上一次伟大革命的观察所得出的结论，在下一次伟大的无产阶级革命到来之际，却被人们遗忘了。

All this was written a little less than half a century ago; and now one has to engage in excavations, as it were, in order to bring undistorted Marxism to the knowledge of the mass of the people. The conclusions drawn from the observation of the last great revolution which Marx lived through were forgotten just when the time for the next great proletarian revolution has arrived.

“……巴黎公社所遭受的多种解读，以及在其中表达的多种利益，都表明它是一种极其灵活的政治形式，而此前所有政体本质上都是压制性的。它的真正秘密在于：它本质上是一个工人阶级政府，是生产阶级反对占有阶级斗争的成果，是最终发现的能够实现劳动者经济解放的政治形式……”

"... The multiplicity of interpretations to which the Commune has been subjected, and the multiplicity of interests which expressed themselves in it show that it was a thoroughly flexible political form, while all previous forms of government had been essentially repressive. Its true secret was this: it was essentially a working-class government, the result of the struggle of the producing against the appropriating class, the political form at last discovered under which the economic emancipation of labor could be accomplished....

“若非满足这最后一个条件，《社群宪法》就根本不可能实现，纯属幻想……”

"Except on this last condition, the Communal Constitution would have been an impossibility and a delusion...."

空想家们忙于“发现”社会主义社会改造所需的政治形式。无政府主义者则完全无视政治形式的问题。当今社会民主党的机会主义者们将议会民主国家的资产阶级政治形式奉为不可逾越的界限；他们为此“模式”顶礼膜拜，并将任何打破这些形式的愿望斥为无政府主义。

The utopians busied themselves with "discovering" political forms under which the socialist transformation of society was to take place. The anarchists dismissed the question of political forms altogether. The opportunists of present-day Social-Democracy accepted the bourgeois political forms of the parliamentary democratic state as the limit which should not be overstepped; they battered their foreheads praying before this "model", and denounced as anarchism every desire to break these forms.

马克思从社会主义和政治斗争的整个历史中推断出，国家必然消亡，而国家消亡的过渡形式（从国家到非国家的过渡）将是“组织起来的无产阶级作为统治阶级”。然而，马克思并没有着手探究这一未来阶段的政治形式。他仅限于仔细观察法国历史，对其进行分析，并得出1851年所导致的结论，即事态正朝着资产阶级国家机器的毁灭发展。

Marx deduced from the whole history of socialism and the political struggle that the state was bound to disappear, and that the transitional form of its disappearance (the transition from state to non-state) would be the "proletariat organized as the ruling class". Marx, however, did not set out to discover the political forms of this future stage. He limited himself to carefully observing French history, to analyzing it, and to drawing the conclusion to which the year 1851 had led, namely, that matters were moving towards destruction of the bourgeois state machine.

当无产阶级群众革命运动爆发时，马克思尽管经历了失败，尽管这场运动短暂且明显软弱，但他还是开始研究这场运动所发现的各种形式。

And when the mass revolutionary movement of the proletariat burst forth, Marx, in spite of its failure, in spite of its short life and patent weakness, began to study the forms it had discovered.

公社是无产阶级革命“最终发现”的一种形式，在这种形式下，劳动者的经济解放才能实现。

The Commune is the form "at last discovered" by the proletarian revolution, under which the economic emancipation of labor can take place.

公社是无产阶级革命第一次尝试摧毁资产阶级国家机器；它是“最终发现的”政治形式，通过这种形式，被摧毁的国家机器可以而且必须被取代。

The Commune is the first attempt by a proletarian revolution to smash the bourgeois state machine; and it is the political form "at last discovered", by which the smashed state machine can and must be replaced.

我们将进一步看到，1905 年和 1917 年的俄国革命，在不同的形势和不同的条件下，延续了巴黎公社的工作，并证实了马克思精辟的历史分析。

We shall see further on that the Russian revolutions of 1905 and 1917, in different circumstances and under different conditions, continue the work of the Commune and confirm Marx's brilliant historical analysis.

恩格斯的补充说明

Supplementary Explanations by Engels

住房问题

争议；与无政府主义者的

争论；致倍倍尔的信；

对埃尔福特纲领草案的批评；

恩格斯论民主的克服

The Housing Question

Controversy with the Anarchists

Letter to Bebel

Criticism of the Draft of the Erfurt Programme

The 1891 Preface to Marx's "The Civil War in France"

Engels on the Overcoming of Democracy

 

 

马克思阐述了公社经验意义的基本原理。恩格斯反复论述这一主题，并阐释马克思的分析和结论，有时他对问题的其他方面阐述得如此有力生动，以至于有必要专门讨论他的阐释。

Marx gave the fundamentals concerning the significance of the experience of the Commune. Engels returned to the same subject time and again, and explained Marx's analysis and conclusions, sometimes elucidating other aspects of the question with such power and vividness that it is necessary to deal with his explanations specially.



 



 

1. 住房问题

1. The Housing Question

恩格斯在其著作《住房问题》（1872年）中已经考虑到了巴黎公社的经验，并多次论述了革命与国家的关系。值得注意的是，他对这一具体问题的论述一方面清晰地揭示了无产阶级国家与现今国家之间的相似之处——这些相似之处使得在两种情况下都应称之为国家——另一方面也揭示了二者之间的差异，或者说，揭示了国家走向毁灭的过渡。

In his work, The Housing Question (1872), Engels already took into account the experience of the Commune, and dealt several times with the tasks of the revolution in relation to the state. It is interesting to note that the treatment of this specific subject clearly revealed, on the one hand, points of similarity between the proletarian state and the present state - points that warrant speaking of the state in both cases - and, on the other hand, points of difference between them, or the transition to the destruction of the state.

那么，住房问题该如何解决呢？在当今社会，它的解决方式与其他社会问题一样：通过经济手段逐步平衡供需关系，而这种解决方式本身又会不断重复出现住房问题，因此根本算不上真正的解决。社会革命如何解决这个问题，不仅取决于具体情况，还与许多更为深远的问题息息相关，其中最根本的问题之一就是消除城乡对立。我们的任务并非为未来的社会组织构建乌托邦式的体系，因此在此探讨这个问题毫无意义。但有一点是肯定的：大城市里现有的住房数量足以立即解决所有真正的“住房短缺”问题，前提是这些住房得到合理利用。而合理利用住房自然只能通过没收现有房主的房屋，并将无家可归的工人或居住拥挤的工人安置其中来实现。一旦无产阶级夺取政权，这种出于公共利益考量的措施将是正当的。与其他国家进行的征用和征用一样容易实施。

"How is the housing question to be settled then? In present-day society, it is settled just as any other social question: by the gradual economic levelling of demand and supply, a settlement which reproduces the question itself again and again and therefore is no settlement. How a social revolution would settle this question not only depends on the circumstances in each particular case, but is also connected with much more far-reaching questions, one of the most fundamental of which is the abolition of the antithesis between town and country. As it is not our task to create utopian systems for the organization of the future society, it would be more than idle to go into the question here. But one thing is certain: there is already a sufficient quantity of houses in the big cities to remedy immediately all real 'housing shortage', provided they are used judiciously. This can naturally only occur through the expropriation of the present owners and by quartering in their houses homeless workers or workers overcrowded in their present homes. As soon as the proletariat has won political power, such a measure prompted by concern for the common good will be just as easy to carry out as are other expropriations and billetings by the present-day state."

（德文版，1887年，第22页）

(German edition, 1887, p.22)

本文不探讨国家权力形式的变化，而只考察其活动内容。即使是现今的国家，也仍然会下令征用和征用房屋。从形式上看，无产阶级国家也会“命令”占领住宅和征用房屋。但显而易见，与资产阶级勾结的旧行政机构——官僚机构——根本无法执行无产阶级国家的命令。

The change in the form of state power is not examined here, but only the content of its activity. Expropriations and billetings take place by order even of the present state. From the formal point of view, the proletarian state will also "order" the occupation of dwellings and expropriation of houses. But it is clear that the old executive apparatus, the bureaucracy, which is connected with the bourgeoisie, would simply be unfit to carry out the orders of the proletarian state.

“……必须指出，劳动人民‘实际占有’所有劳动工具，即劳动人民整体接管工业，与普鲁东主义的‘赎回’截然相反。在后一种情况下，个体劳动者成为住房、农场和劳动工具的所有者；而在前一种情况下，“劳动人民”仍然是房屋、工厂和劳动工具的集体所有者，并且至少在过渡时期内，他们几乎不会允许个人或团体在未获得补偿的情况下使用这些工具。同样，废除土地所有制并非废除地租，而是将其以某种形式转移给社会。因此，劳动人民实际占有所有劳动工具，丝毫不会排除保留地租关系的可能性。”

"... It must be pointed out that the 'actual seizure' of all the instruments of labor, the taking possession of industry as a whole by the working people, is the exact opposite of the Proudhonist 'redemption'. In the latter case the individual worker becomes the owner of the dwelling, the peasant farm, the instruments of labor; in the former case, the 'working people' remain the collective owners of the houses, factories and instruments of labor, and will hardly permit their use, at least during a transitional period, by individuals or associations without compensation for the cost. In the same way, the abolition of property in land is not the abolition of ground rent but its transfer, if in a modified form, to society. The actual seizure of all the instruments of labor by the working people, therefore, does not at all preclude the retention of rent relations."

（第68页）

(p.68)

我们将在下一章探讨这段文字中提及的问题，即国家消亡的经济基础。恩格斯措辞极为谨慎，他说无产阶级国家“至少在过渡时期”不会“允许”人们无偿使用房屋。将全人民拥有的房屋出租给各个家庭，就意味着要收取租金，进行一定程度的监管，并在分配住房时采用某种标准。所有这些都需要某种形式的国家，但绝不需要一个特殊的军事官僚机构，更不需要官员占据特殊特权。要过渡到能够免费提供住房的局面，就取决于国家的彻底“消亡”。

We shall examine the question touched upon in this passage, namely, the economic basis for the withering away of the state, in the next chapter. Engels expresses himself most cautiously. saying that the proletarian state would "hardly" permit the use of houses without payment, "at least during a transitional period". The letting of houses owed by the whole people to individual families presupposes the collection of rent, a certain amount of control, nd the employment of some standard in allotting the housing. All this calls for a certain form of state, but it does not at all call for a special military bureaucratic apparatus, with officials occupying especially privileged positions. The transition to a situation in which it will be possible to supply dwellings rent-free depends on the complete "withering away" of the state.

谈到布朗基主义者在巴黎公社之后，受其经验影响而接受马克思主义基本立场时，恩格斯顺便对这一立场作了如下表述：

Speaking of the Blanquists' adoption of the fundamental position of Marxism after the Commune and under the influence of its experience, Engels, in passing, formulates this position as follows:

“……无产阶级采取政治行动及其专政的必要性，是向消灭阶级以及随之消灭国家的过渡……”

"... Necessity of political action by the proletariat and of its dictatorship as the transition to the abolition of classes and, with them, of the state...."

（第55页）

(p.55)

那些热衷于吹毛求疵批评的人，或者资产阶级“马克思主义消灭者”，或许会在上述《反杜林》的段落中看到这样的矛盾：一方面承认“废除国家”，另一方面又否定这一论断是无政府主义的。如果机会主义者也把恩格斯归类为“无政府主义者”，那也并不奇怪，因为社会沙文主义者指责国际主义者是无政府主义者的做法越来越普遍。

Addicts of hair-splitting criticism, or bourgeois "exterminators of Marxism", will perhaps see a contradiction between this recognition of the "abolition of the state" and repudiation of this formula as an anarchist one in the above passage from Anti-Dühring. It would not be surprising if the opportunists classed Engels, too, as an "anarchist", for it is becoming increasingly common with the social-chauvinists to accuse the internationalists of anarchism.

马克思主义一直认为，随着阶级的消灭，国家也必将消亡。《反杜林论》中关于“国家消亡”的著名段落，不仅指责无政府主义者赞成废除国家，而且还鼓吹国家可以“一夜之间”被废除。

Marxism has always taught that with the abolition of classes the state will also be abolished. The well-known passage on the "withering away of the state in Anti-Dühring accuses the anarchists not simply of favoring the abolition of the state, but of preaching that the state can be abolished "overnight".

由于现在盛行的“社会民主主义”理论完全歪曲了马克思主义与无政府主义在废除国家问题上的关系，因此回顾马克思和恩格斯反对无政府主义者的那场争论将特别有用。

As the now prevailing "Social-Democratic" doctrine completely distorts the relation of Marxism to anarchism on the question of the abolition of the state, it will be particularly useful to recall a certain controversy in which Marx and Engels came out against the anarchists.



 



 

与无政府主义者的争议

Controversy with the Anarchists

这场争论发生在1873年。马克思和恩格斯为意大利的一份社会主义年刊撰写文章，抨击蒲鲁东主义者、“自治主义者”或“反权威主义者”。直到1913年，这些文章才以德文形式发表在《新时代周报》上。

This controversy took place in 1873. Marx and Engels contributed articles against the Proudhonists, "autonomists" or "anti- authoritarians", to an Italian socialist annual, and it was not until 1913 that these articles appeared in German in Neue Zeit

“如果工人阶级的政治斗争采取革命形式，”马克思写道，他嘲笑无政府主义者拒绝政治，“如果工人阶级建立革命专政来取代资产阶级专政，他们就犯下了违背原则的可怕罪行，因为为了满足他们卑劣庸俗的日常需要，为了镇压资产阶级的抵抗，他们给国家赋予了革命的、暂时的形式，而不是放下武器，废除国家。”

"If the political struggle of the working class assumes revolutionary form," wrote Marx, ridiculing the anarchists for their repudiation of politics, "and if the workers set up their revolutionary dictatorship in place of the dictatorship of the bourgeoisie, they commit the terrible crime of violating principles, for in order to satisfy their wretched, vulgar everyday needs and to crush the resistance of the bourgeoisie, they give the state a revolutionary and transient form, instead of laying down their arms and abolishing the state."

（《新时代》第 XXXII 卷，1，1913-14，第 40 页）

(Neue Zeit Vol.XXXII, 1, 1913-14, p.40)

马克思反驳无政府主义者，正是反对这种“废除”国家的做法！他丝毫不反对阶级消失时国家也会消失，或者阶级消失时国家也会被废除的观点。他反对的是工人应该放弃使用武器、放弃有组织的暴力，也就是放弃国家，因为国家的作用是“镇压资产阶级的抵抗”。

It was solely against this kind of "abolition" of the state that Marx fought in refuting the anarchists! He did not at all oppose the view that the state would disappear when classes disappeared, or that it would be abolished when classes were abolished. What he did oppose was the proposition that the workers should renounce the use of arms, organized violence, that is, the state, which is to serve to "crush the resistance of the bourgeoisie".

为了防止他反对无政府主义的斗争的真正意义被歪曲，马克思明确强调了无产阶级需要的国家的“革命的、暂时的形式”。无产阶级对国家的需要只是暂时的。毕竟，在废除国家作为最终目标的问题上，我们与无政府主义者并没有分歧。我们认为，为了实现这一目标，我们必须暂时利用国家政权的工具、资源和方法来对抗剥削者，正如被压迫阶级的暂时专政对于消灭阶级是必要的一样。马克思选择了最尖锐、最清晰的方式来阐述他对无政府主义者的批判：工人在推翻资本家的枷锁之后，难道应该“放下武器”，还是应该用武器来镇压资本家的抵抗？一个阶级系统地使用武器对抗另一个阶级，这难道不是一种“暂时的形式”的国家吗？

To prevent the true meaning of his struggle against anarchism from being distorted, Marx expressly emphasized the "revolutionary and transient form" of the state which the proletariat needs. The proletariat needs the state only temporarily. We do not after all differ with the anarchists on the question of the abolition of the state as the aim. We maintain that, to achieve this aim, we must temporarily make use of the instruments, resources, and methods of state power against the exploiters, just as the temporary dictatorship of the oppressed class is necessary for the abolition of classes. Marx chooses the sharpest and clearest way of stating his case against the anarchists: After overthrowing the yoke of the capitalists, should the workers "lay down their arms", or use them against the capitalists in order to crush their resistance? But what is the systematic use of arms by ne class against another if not a "transient form" of state?

每个社会民主党人都应该扪心自问：他与无政府主义者争论国家问题时，是否就是这样提出的？第二国际绝大多数官方社会主义政党是否也是这样提出的？

Let every Social-Democrat ask himself: Is that how he has been posing the question of the state in controversy with the anarchists? Is that how it has been posed by the vast majority of the official socialist parties of the Second International?

恩格斯以更详尽、更通俗易懂的方式阐述了同样的思想。首先，他嘲讽了蒲鲁东主义者的混乱思想，他们自称为“反权威主义者”，即否定一切权威、一切服从、一切权力。恩格斯说，以工厂、铁路、远洋轮船为例：难道不清楚，这些基于机器运转和众多人员系统合作的复杂技术机构，如果没有一定程度的服从，因而也必然存在一定程度的权威或权力，就无法正常运作吗？

Engels expounds the same ideas in much greater detail and still more popularly. First of all he ridicules the muddled ideas of the Proudhonists, who call themselves "anti-authoritarians", i.e., repudiated all authority, all subordination, all power. Take a factory, a railway, a ship on the high seas, said Engels: is it not clear that not one of these complex technical establishments, based on the use of machinery and the systematic co-operation of many people, could function without a certain amount of subordination and, consequently, without a certain amount of authority or power?

“……当我用这些论点反驳那些最激进的反权威主义者时，他们唯一能给出的回答是：哦，没错，但这里的问题不是我们赋予代表的权力，而是委员会！这些人以为改个名字就能改变事物本身……”

"... When I counter the most rabid anti-authoritarians with these arguments, they only answer they can give me is the following: Oh, that's true, except that here it is not a question of authority with which we vest our delegates, but of a commission! These people imagine they can change a thing by changing its name...."

恩格斯由此表明，权威和自主是相对的，它们的适用范围随着社会发展的各个阶段而变化，把它们当作绝对的东西是荒谬的，并且机器和大规模生产的应用范围也在不断扩大，于是他从对权威的一般性讨论转向了国家问题。

Having thus shown that authority and autonomy are relative terms, that the sphere of their application varies with the various phases of social development, that it is absurd to take them as absolutes, and adding that the sphere of application of machinery and large-scale production is steadily expanding, Engels passes from the general discussion of authority to the question of the state.

他写道：“如果自治主义者们满足于说，未来的社会组织只会允许权威存在于生产条件必然决定的范围内，那么人们或许还能与他们达成共识。但他们对所有使权威成为必要的事实视而不见，并且激烈地反对权威这个词。”

"Had the autonomists," he wrote, "contented themselves with saying that the social organization of the future would allow authority only within the bounds which the conditions of production make inevitable, one could have come to terms with them. But they are blind to all facts that make authority necessary and they passionately fight the word.

为什么反威权主义者不仅限于反对政治权威和国家呢？所有社会主义者都一致认为，随着即将到来的社会革命，国家及其政治权威将会消失，也就是说，公共职能将失去其政治性质，而沦为单纯的监督社会利益的行政职能。但是，反威权主义者却要求在维系政治国家的社会关系尚未被摧毁之前，就一举废除政治国家。他们要求社会革命的第一步就是废除权威。

"Why do the anti-authoritarians not confine themselves to crying out against political authority, the state? All socialists are agreed that the state, and with it political authority, will disappear as a result of the coming social revolution, that is, that public functions will lose their political character and become mere administrative functions of watching over social interests. But the anti-authoritarians demand that the political state be abolished at one stroke, even before the social relations that gave both to it have been destroyed. They demand that the first act of the social revolution shall be the abolition of authority.

“这些先生们见过革命吗？革命无疑是最专制的；它是一部分人民用步枪、刺刀和大炮等高度专制的手段，将自己的意志强加于另一部分人民的行为。胜利的一方必须依靠其武器在反动派中造成的恐怖来维持统治。如果巴黎公社没有利用武装人民的权威来对抗资产阶级，它能持续超过一天吗？难道我们不应该反过来指责它没有充分利用这种权威吗？因此，只有两种可能：要么反权威主义者根本不知道自己在说什么，在这种情况下，他们只会制造混乱；要么他们确实知道，在这种情况下，他们是在背叛无产阶级的事业。无论哪种情况，他们都只会为反动派服务。”

"Have these gentlemen ever seen a revolution? A revolution is certainly the most authoritarian thing there is; it is an act whereby one part of the population imposes its will upon the other part by means of rifles, bayonets and cannon, all of which are highly authoritarian means. And the victorious party must maintain its rule by means of the terror which its arms inspire in the reactionaries. Would the Paris Commune have lasted more than a day if it had not used the authority of the armed people against the bourgeoisie? Cannot we, on the contrary, blame it for having made too little use of that authority? Therefore, one of two things: either that anti-authoritarians down't know what they are talking about, in which case they are creating nothing but confusion. Or they do know, and in that case they are betraying the cause of the proletariat. In either case they serve only reaction."

（第39页）

(p.39)

这一论点触及了在国家消亡过程中政治与经济关系方面需要探讨的问题（下一章将专门讨论这个问题）。这些问题包括：公共职能从政治职能向简单行政职能的转变，以及“政治国家”的概念。最后一个术语尤其容易被误解，它指的是国家消亡的过程：在这一过程的某个阶段，正在消亡的国家可以被称为非政治国家。

This argument touches upon questions which should be examined in connection with the relationship between politics and economics during the withering away of the state (the next chapter is devoted to this). These questions are: the transformation of public functions from political into simple functions of administration, and the "political state". This last term, one particularly liable to misunderstanding, indicates the process of the withering away of the state: at a certain stage of this process, the state which is withering away may be called a non-political state.

恩格斯这一论证中最引人注目之处在于他驳斥无政府主义者的方式。自称是恩格斯门徒的社会民主党人，自1873年以来就此问题与无政府主义者进行了无数次辩论，但他们的论证方式却远不及马克思主义者所能及和应有的方式。恩格斯指出，无政府主义者废除国家的思想是混乱的、非革命性的。无政府主义者恰恰忽视了革命的兴起和发展，以及革命在暴力、权威、权力、国家等方面的具体任务。

Against, the most remarkable thing in this argument of Engels' is the way he states his case against the anarchists. Social-Democrats, claiming to be disciples of Engels, have argued on this subject against the anarchists millions of times since 1873, but they have not argued as Marxists could and should. The anarchist idea of abolition of the state is muddled and non-revolutionary - that is how Engels put it. It is precisely the revolution in its rise and development, with its specific tasks in relation to violence, authority, power, the state, that the anarchists refuse to see.

当今社会民主党人对无政府主义的惯常批评，归根结底不过是最庸俗的陈词滥调：“我们承认国家，而无政府主义者不承认！” 这种陈词滥调自然会令那些有思考能力和革命思想的工人感到反感。恩格斯的观点则截然不同。他强调，所有社会主义者都认识到，国家终将随着社会主义革命的结束而消亡。随后，他专门探讨了革命问题——这个问题，社会民主党人通常出于机会主义而回避，仿佛完全留给了无政府主义者去“解决”。在探讨这个问题时，恩格斯直面问题；他问道：巴黎公社难道不应该更多地利用国家的革命力量，也就是利用武装起来、组织起来的无产阶级作为统治阶级的力量吗？

The usual criticism of anarchism by present-day Social-Democrats has boiled down to the purest philistine banality: "We recognize the state, whereas the anarchists do not!" Naturally, such banality cannot but repel workers who are at all capable of thinking and revolutionary-minded. What Engels says is different. He stresses that all socialists recognize that the state will disappear as a result of the socialist revolution. He then deals specifically with the question of the revolution - the very question which, as a rule, the Social-Democrats evade out of opportunism, leaving it, so to speak, exclusively for the anarchists "to work out". And when dealing with this question, Engels takes the bull by the horns; he asks: should not the Commune have made more use of the revolutionary power of the state, that is, of the proletariat armed and organized as the ruling class?

当时盛行的官方社会民主党通常对无产阶级在革命中的具体任务不屑一顾，要么以庸俗的嘲讽，要么充其量用诡辩的回避语搪塞：“将来会证明一切。”无政府主义者有理由指责这些社会民主党人未能尽到对工人进行革命教育的职责。恩格斯借鉴上次无产阶级革命的经验，正是为了具体研究无产阶级应该做什么，以及应该如何做，尤其是在与银行和国家的关系方面。

Prevailing official Social-Democracy usually dismissed the question of the concrete tasks of the proletariat in the revolution either with a philistine sneer, or, at best, with the sophistic evasion: "The future will show". And the anarchists were justified in saying about such Social-Democrats that they were failing in their task of giving the workers a revolutionary education. Engels draws upon the experience of the last proletarian revolution precisely for the purpose of making a most concrete study of what should be done by the proletariat, and in what manner, in relation to both the banks and the state.



 



 

致倍倍尔的信

Letter to Bebel

在马克思和恩格斯的著作中，关于国家最引人注目的论述之一，即使不是最引人注目的，也包含在恩格斯于1875年3月18日至28日写给倍倍尔的信中的以下段落中。我们不妨在括号中指出，据我们所知，这封信最初是由倍倍尔发表在他1911年出版的回忆录第二卷（《我的生活》）中的，也就是说，这封信是在36年前写成并寄出的。

One of the most, if not the most, remarkable observation on the state in the works of Marx and Engels is contained in the following passage in Engels' letter to Bebel dated March 18-28, 1875. This letter, we may observe in parenthesis, was, as far as we know, first published by Bebel in the second volume of his memoirs (Aus meinem Leben), which appeared in 1911, i.e., 36 years after the letter had been written and sent.

恩格斯致信倍倍尔，批评了马克思在著名的致布拉克信中批评过的同一份《哥达纲领》草案。恩格斯特别针对国家问题指出：

Engels wrote to Bebel criticizing the same draft of the Gotha Programme which Marx criticized in his famous letter to Bracke. Referring specially to the question of the state, Engels said:

“自由人民的国家已经演变成自由国家。从语法意义上讲，自由国家是指国家相对于其公民而言是自由的，因此也指拥有专制政府的国家。关于国家的一切讨论都应该停止，尤其是在巴黎公社之后，因为巴黎公社在严格意义上已经不再是一个国家了。无政府主义者把‘人民国家’这个概念强加给我们，令人作呕，尽管马克思在《反蒲鲁东》一书中以及后来的《共产党宣言》中都明确指出，随着社会主义社会秩序的建立，国家会自行解体（sich auflost）并消失。既然国家只是一个过渡性的机构，在斗争和革命中被用来以武力镇压对手，那么谈论‘自由人民的国家’就纯属无稽之谈；只要无产阶级仍然需要国家，那么他们需要国家并非为了自由，而是为了镇压对手。”一旦自由成为可能，国家本身也就不复存在了。因此，我们建议用“Gemeinwesen”（德语，意为“共同体”）一词取代所有“国家”一词。“Gemeinwesen ”是一个古老的德语词汇，完全可以替代法语中的“commune”（公社）。

"The free people's state has been transferred into the free state. Taken in its grammatical sense, a free state is one where the state is free in relation to its citizens, hence a state with a despotic government. The whole talk about the state should be dropped, especially since the Commune, which was no longer a state in the proper sense of the word. The 'people's state' has been thrown in our faces by the anarchists to the point of disgust, although already Marx's book against Proudhon and later the Communist Manifesto say plainly that with the introduction of the socialist order of society the state dissolves of itself [sich auflost] and disappears. As the state is only a transitional institution which is used in the struggle, in the revolution, to hold down one's adversaries by force, it is sheer nonsense to talk of a 'free people's state'; so long as the proletariat still needs the state, it does not need it in the interests of freedom but in order to hold down its adversaries, and as soon as it becomes possible to speak of freedom the state as such ceases to exist. We would therefore propose replacing the state everywhere by Gemeinwesen, a good old German word which can very well take the place of the French word commune."

（德文原著第321-322页）

(pp.321-22 of the German original)

应当注意的是，这封信指的是马克思在几周后写的另一封信中批评过的党纲（马克思的信写于1875年5月5日），而且当时恩格斯正与马克思一起住在伦敦。因此，当恩格斯在最后一句中使用“我们”时，无疑是以他自己以及马克思的名义，向德国工人党的领袖建议，将党纲中的“国家”一词删除，代之以“共同体”。

It should be borne in mind that this letter refers to the party programme which Marx criticized in a letter dated only a few weeks later than the above (Marx's letter is dated May 5, 1875), and that at the time Engels was living with Marx in London. Consequently, when he says "we" in the last sentence, Engels undoubtedly, in his own as well as in Marx's name, suggests to the leader of the German workers' party that the word "state" be struck out of the programme and replaced by the word "community".

如果向当今被投机分子歪曲的“马克思主义”的领军人物提出这样的纲领修改建议，他们一定会对“无政府主义”发出多么强烈的抗议啊！

What a howl about "anarchism" would be raised by the leading lights of present-day "Marxism", which has been falsified for the convenience of the opportunists, if such an amendment of the programme were suggested to them!

让他们嚎叫吧。这将为他们赢得资产阶级的赞扬。

Let them howl. This will earn them the praises of the bourgeoisie.

我们将继续我们的工作。在修订我们党的纲领时，我们必须务必考虑恩格斯和马克思的建议，以便更接近真理，通过消除歪曲来恢复马克思主义，更正确地指导工人阶级争取解放的斗争。布尔什维克中肯定没有人会反对恩格斯和马克思的建议。唯一可能出现的困难是关于“共同体”这个词。德语中有两个词表示“共同体”，恩格斯使用的是其中一个，它指的不是单个共同体，而是所有共同体的总和，一个共同体体系。俄语中没有这样的词，我们可能不得不选择法语词“commune”，尽管这个词也有它的不足之处。

And we shall go on with our work. In revising the programme of our Party, we must by all means take the advice of Engels and Marx into consideration in order to come nearer the truth, to restore Marxism by ridding it of distortions, to guide the struggle of the working class for its emancipation more correctly. Certainly no one opposed to the advice of Engels and Marx will be found among the Bolsheviks. The only difficulty that may perhaps arise will be in regard to the term. In German there are two words meaning "community", of which Engels used the one which does not denote a single community, but their totality, a system of communities. In Russian there is no such word, and we may have to choose the French word "commune", although this also has its drawbacks.

“公社不再是严格意义上的国家了”——这是恩格斯提出的最具理论意义的论断。在前面论述之后，这一论断就显得非常清晰了。公社不再是国家，因为它必须镇压的不是大多数民众，而是少数人（剥削者）。它摧毁了资产阶级国家机器。民众自身取代了特殊的强制力量。这一切都标志着公社脱离了严格意义上的国家。如果公社稳固建立起来，其中所有国家的痕迹都会自行“消亡”；它无需“废除”国家机构——这些机构会停止运作，因为它们已经失去了存在的意义。

"The Commune was no longer a state in the proper sense of the word" - this is the most theoretically important statement Engels makes. After what has been said above, this statement is perfectly clear. The Commune was ceasing to be a state since it had to suppress, not the majority of the population, but a minority (the exploiters). It had smashed the bourgeois state machine. In place of a special coercive force the population itself came on the scene. All this was a departure from the state in the proper sense of the word. And had the Commune become firmly established, all traces of the state in it would have "withered away" of themselves; it would not have had to "abolish" the institutions of the state - they would have ceased to function as they ceased to have anything to do.

“‘人民国家’这个概念被无政府主义者抛到我们面前。”恩格斯说这番话时，首先想到的是巴枯宁及其对德国社会民主党的攻击。恩格斯承认，这些攻击是合理的，因为“人民国家”和“自由人民国家”一样荒谬，都背离了社会主义。恩格斯试图引导德国社会民主党人与无政府主义者的斗争走上正轨，使这场斗争在原则上正确，并使其摆脱对“国家”的投机偏见。不幸的是，恩格斯的这封信被束之高阁长达36年之久。我们将在后文中看到，即使在这封信发表之后，考茨基仍然坚持犯着几乎与恩格斯警告过的错误相同的错误。

"The 'people's state' has been thrown in our faces by the anarchists". In saying this, Engels above all has in mind Bakunin and his attacks on the German Social-Democrats. Engels admits that these attacks were justified insofar as the "people's state" was as much an absurdity and as much a departure from socialism as the "free people's state".
